106//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
107// [SECTION] STB libraries implementation (for stb_truetype and stb_rect_pack)
108//-------------------------------------------------------------------------
109
110// Compile time options:
111// #define IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE ImStb
112// #define IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_truetype.h"
113// #define IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_rect_pack.h"
114// #define IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
115// #define IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION
116
117#ifdef IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
118namespace IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
119{
120#endif
121
122#ifdef _MSC_VER
123#pragma warning(push)
124#pragma warning(disable : 4456) // declaration of 'xx' hides previous local declaration
125#pragma warning(disable : 6011) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer 'cur->next'.
126#pragma warning(disable : 6385) // (stb_truetype) Reading invalid data from 'buffer': the readable size is
127 // '_Old_3`kernel_width' bytes, but '3' bytes may be read.
128#pragma warning( \
129 disable \
130 : 28182) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer. 'cur' contains the same NULL value as 'cur->next' did.
131#endif
132
133#if defined(__clang__)
134#pragma clang diagnostic push
135#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wunused-function" // warning: 'xxxx' defined but not used
136#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wmissing-prototypes"
137#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wimplicit-fallthrough"
138#endif
139
140#if defined(__GNUC__)
141#pragma GCC diagnostic push
142#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored \
143 "-Wtype-limits" // warning: comparison is always true due to limited range of data type [-Wtype-limits]
144#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored "-Wimplicit-fallthrough" // warning: this statement may fall through
145#endif
146
147#ifndef STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit
148 // (e.g. unity builds)
149#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another
150 // compilation unit
151#define STBRP_STATIC
152#define STBRP_ASSERT(x) \
153 do \
154 { \
155 IM_ASSERT(x); \
156 } while (0)
157#define STBRP_SORT ImQsort
158#define STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION
159#endif
160#ifdef IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
161#include IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
162#else
163#include "imstb_rectpack.h"
164#endif
165#endif
166
167#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
168#ifndef STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit
169 // (e.g. unity builds)
170#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another
171 // compilation unit
172#define STBTT_malloc(x, u) ((void)(u), IM_ALLOC(x))
173#define STBTT_free(x, u) ((void)(u), IM_FREE(x))
174#define STBTT_assert(x) \
175 do \
176 { \
177 IM_ASSERT(x); \
178 } while (0)
179#define STBTT_fmod(x, y) ImFmod(x, y)
180#define STBTT_sqrt(x) ImSqrt(x)
181#define STBTT_pow(x, y) ImPow(x, y)
182#define STBTT_fabs(x) ImFabs(x)
183#define STBTT_ifloor(x) ((int)ImFloor(x))
184#define STBTT_iceil(x) ((int)ImCeil(x))
185#define STBTT_strlen(x) ImStrlen(x)
186#define STBTT_STATIC
187#define STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
188#else
189#define STBTT_DEF extern
190#endif
191#ifdef IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
192#include IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
193#else
194#include "imstb_truetype.h"
195#endif
196#endif
197#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
198
199#if defined(__GNUC__)

201#endif

205#endif

352// Those light colors are better suited with a thicker font than the default one + FrameBorder
353void ImGui::StyleColorsLight(ImGuiStyle *dst)
354{
355 ImGuiStyle *style = dst ? dst : &ImGui::GetStyle();
356 ImVec4 *colors = style->Colors;
357
358 colors[ImGuiCol_Text] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 1.00f);
359 colors[ImGuiCol_TextDisabled] = ImVec4(0.60f, 0.60f, 0.60f, 1.00f);
360 colors[ImGuiCol_WindowBg] = ImVec4(0.94f, 0.94f, 0.94f, 1.00f);
361 colors[ImGuiCol_ChildBg] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f);
362 colors[ImGuiCol_PopupBg] = ImVec4(1.00f, 1.00f, 1.00f, 0.98f);
363 colors[ImGuiCol_Border] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.30f);
364 colors[ImGuiCol_BorderShadow] = ImVec4(0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f, 0.00f);

419//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
420// [SECTION] ImDrawList
421//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
422
423ImDrawListSharedData::ImDrawListSharedData()
424{
425 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
426 InitialFringeScale = 1.0f;
427 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx); i++)
428 {
429 const float a = ((float)i * 2 * IM_PI) / (float)IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx);
430 ArcFastVtx[i] = ImVec2(ImCos(a), ImSin(a));
431 }
432 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
433}
434
435void ImDrawListSharedData::SetCircleTessellationMaxError(float max_error)
436{
437 if (CircleSegmentMaxError == max_error)
438 return;
439
440 IM_ASSERT(max_error > 0.0f);
441 CircleSegmentMaxError = max_error;
442 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(CircleSegmentCounts); i++)
443 {
444 const float radius = (float)i;
445 CircleSegmentCounts[i] = (ImU8)((i > 0) ? IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, CircleSegmentMaxError)
446 : IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX);
447 }
448 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
449}
450
451ImDrawList::ImDrawList(ImDrawListSharedData *shared_data)
452{
453 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
454 _Data = shared_data;
455}
456
457ImDrawList::~ImDrawList()
458{
459 _ClearFreeMemory();
460}
461
462// Initialize before use in a new frame. We always have a command ready in the buffer.
463// In the majority of cases, you would want to call PushClipRect() and PushTextureID() after this.
464void ImDrawList::_ResetForNewFrame()
465{
466 // Verify that the ImDrawCmd fields we want to memcmp() are contiguous in memory.
467 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, ClipRect) == 0);
468 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, TextureId) == sizeof(ImVec4));
469 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) == sizeof(ImVec4) + sizeof(ImTextureID));
470 if (_Splitter._Count > 1)
471 _Splitter.Merge(this);
472
473 CmdBuffer.resize(0);
474 IdxBuffer.resize(0);
475 VtxBuffer.resize(0);
476 Flags = _Data->InitialFlags;
477 memset(&_CmdHeader, 0, sizeof(_CmdHeader));
478 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
479 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
480 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
481 _ClipRectStack.resize(0);
482 _TextureIdStack.resize(0);
483 _CallbacksDataBuf.resize(0);
484 _Path.resize(0);
485 _Splitter.Clear();
486 CmdBuffer.push_back(ImDrawCmd());
487 _FringeScale = _Data->InitialFringeScale;
488}
489
490void ImDrawList::_ClearFreeMemory()
491{
492 CmdBuffer.clear();
493 IdxBuffer.clear();
494 VtxBuffer.clear();
495 Flags = ImDrawListFlags_None;
496 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
497 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
498 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
499 _ClipRectStack.clear();
500 _TextureIdStack.clear();
501 _CallbacksDataBuf.clear();
502 _Path.clear();
503 _Splitter.ClearFreeMemory();
504}
505
506ImDrawList *ImDrawList::CloneOutput() const
507{
508 ImDrawList *dst = IM_NEW(ImDrawList(_Data));
509 dst->CmdBuffer = CmdBuffer;
510 dst->IdxBuffer = IdxBuffer;
511 dst->VtxBuffer = VtxBuffer;
512 dst->Flags = Flags;
513 return dst;
514}
515
516void ImDrawList::AddDrawCmd()
517{
518 ImDrawCmd draw_cmd;
519 draw_cmd.ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect; // Same as calling ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy()
520 draw_cmd.TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
521 draw_cmd.VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
522 draw_cmd.IdxOffset = IdxBuffer.Size;
523
524 IM_ASSERT(draw_cmd.ClipRect.x <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.z && draw_cmd.ClipRect.y <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.w);
525 CmdBuffer.push_back(draw_cmd);
526}
527
528// Pop trailing draw command (used before merging or presenting to user)
529// Note that this leaves the ImDrawList in a state unfit for further commands, as most code assume that CmdBuffer.Size >
530// 0 && CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL
531void ImDrawList::_PopUnusedDrawCmd()
532{
533 while (CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
534 {
535 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
536 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 || curr_cmd->UserCallback != NULL)
537 return; // break;
538 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
539 }
540}
541
542void ImDrawList::AddCallback(ImDrawCallback callback, void *userdata, size_t userdata_size)
543{
544 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
545 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
546 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
547 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
548 {
549 AddDrawCmd();
550 curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
551 }
552
553 curr_cmd->UserCallback = callback;
554 if (userdata_size == 0)
555 {
556 // Store user data directly in command (no indirection)
557 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = userdata;
558 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataSize = 0;
559 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset = -1;
560 }
561 else
562 {
563 // Copy and store user data in a buffer
564 IM_ASSERT(userdata != NULL);
565 IM_ASSERT(userdata_size < (1u << 31));
566 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = NULL; // Will be resolved during Render()
567 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataSize = (int)userdata_size;
568 curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset = _CallbacksDataBuf.Size;
569 _CallbacksDataBuf.resize(_CallbacksDataBuf.Size + (int)userdata_size);
570 memcpy(_CallbacksDataBuf.Data + (size_t)curr_cmd->UserCallbackDataOffset, userdata, userdata_size);
571 }
572
573 AddDrawCmd(); // Force a new command after us (see comment below)
574}
575
576// Compare ClipRect, TextureId and VtxOffset with a single memcmp()
577#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize (offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) + sizeof(unsigned int))
578#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS) \
579 (memcmp(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Compare ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
580#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC) \
581 (memcpy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
582#define ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(CMD_0, CMD_1) (CMD_0->IdxOffset + CMD_0->ElemCount == CMD_1->IdxOffset)
583
584// Try to merge two last draw commands
585void ImDrawList::_TryMergeDrawCmds()
586{
587 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
588 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
589 ImDrawCmd *prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
590 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) &&
591 curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
592 {
593 prev_cmd->ElemCount += curr_cmd->ElemCount;
594 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
595 }
596}
597
598// Our scheme may appears a bit unusual, basically we want the most-common calls AddLine AddRect etc. to not have to
599// perform any check so we always have a command ready in the stack. The cost of figuring out if a new command has to be
600// added or if we can merge is paid in those Update** functions only.
601void ImDrawList::_OnChangedClipRect()
602{
603 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
604 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
605 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
606 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && memcmp(&curr_cmd->ClipRect, &_CmdHeader.ClipRect, sizeof(ImVec4)) != 0)
607 {
608 AddDrawCmd();
609 return;
610 }
611 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
612
613 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
614 ImDrawCmd *prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
615 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 &&
616 ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
617 {
618 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
619 return;
620 }
621 curr_cmd->ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
622}
623
624void ImDrawList::_OnChangedTextureID()
625{
626 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
627 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
628 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
629 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && curr_cmd->TextureId != _CmdHeader.TextureId)
630 {
631 AddDrawCmd();
632 return;
633 }
634 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
635
636 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
637 ImDrawCmd *prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
638 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 &&
639 ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
640 {
641 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
642 return;
643 }
644 curr_cmd->TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
645}
646
647void ImDrawList::_OnChangedVtxOffset()
648{
649 // We don't need to compare curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset because we know it'll be different at the
650 // time we call this.
651 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
652 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
653 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
654 // IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset); // See #3349
655 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
656 {
657 AddDrawCmd();
658 return;
659 }
660 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
661 curr_cmd->VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
662}
663
664int ImDrawList::_CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(float radius) const
665{
666 // Automatic segment count
667 const int radius_idx = (int)(radius + 0.999999f); // ceil to never reduce accuracy
668 if (radius_idx >= 0 && radius_idx < IM_ARRAYSIZE(_Data->CircleSegmentCounts))
669 return _Data->CircleSegmentCounts[radius_idx]; // Use cached value
670 else
671 return IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, _Data->CircleSegmentMaxError);
672}
673
674// Render-level scissoring. This is passed down to your render function but not used for CPU-side coarse clipping.
675// Prefer using higher-level ImGui::PushClipRect() to affect logic (hit-testing and widget culling)
676void ImDrawList::PushClipRect(const ImVec2 &cr_min, const ImVec2 &cr_max, bool intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
677{
678 ImVec4 cr(cr_min.x, cr_min.y, cr_max.x, cr_max.y);
679 if (intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
680 {
681 ImVec4 current = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
682 if (cr.x < current.x)
683 cr.x = current.x;
684 if (cr.y < current.y)
685 cr.y = current.y;
686 if (cr.z > current.z)
687 cr.z = current.z;
688 if (cr.w > current.w)
689 cr.w = current.w;
690 }
691 cr.z = ImMax(cr.x, cr.z);
692 cr.w = ImMax(cr.y, cr.w);
693
694 _ClipRectStack.push_back(cr);
695 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = cr;
696 _OnChangedClipRect();
697}
698
699void ImDrawList::PushClipRectFullScreen()
700{
701 PushClipRect(ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.x, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.y),
702 ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.z, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.w));
703}
704
705void ImDrawList::PopClipRect()
706{
707 _ClipRectStack.pop_back();
708 _CmdHeader.ClipRect =
709 (_ClipRectStack.Size == 0) ? _Data->ClipRectFullscreen : _ClipRectStack.Data[_ClipRectStack.Size - 1];
710 _OnChangedClipRect();
711}
712
713void ImDrawList::PushTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
714{
715 _TextureIdStack.push_back(texture_id);
716 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
717 _OnChangedTextureID();
718}
719
720void ImDrawList::PopTextureID()
721{
722 _TextureIdStack.pop_back();
723 _CmdHeader.TextureId =
724 (_TextureIdStack.Size == 0) ? (ImTextureID)NULL : _TextureIdStack.Data[_TextureIdStack.Size - 1];
725 _OnChangedTextureID();
726}
727
728// This is used by ImGui::PushFont()/PopFont(). It works because we never use _TextureIdStack[] elsewhere than in
729// PushTextureID()/PopTextureID().
730void ImDrawList::_SetTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
731{
732 if (_CmdHeader.TextureId == texture_id)
733 return;
734 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
735 _OnChangedTextureID();
736}
737
738// Reserve space for a number of vertices and indices.
739// You must finish filling your reserved data before calling PrimReserve() again, as it may reallocate or
740// submit the intermediate results. PrimUnreserve() can be used to release unused allocations.
741void ImDrawList::PrimReserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
742{
743 // Large mesh support (when enabled)
744 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
745 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 && (_VtxCurrentIdx + vtx_count >= (1 << 16)) && (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
746 {
747 // FIXME: In theory we should be testing that vtx_count <64k here.
748 // In practice, RenderText() relies on reserving ahead for a worst case scenario so it is currently useful for
749 // us to not make that check until we rework the text functions to handle clipping and large horizontal lines
750 // better.
751 _CmdHeader.VtxOffset = VtxBuffer.Size;
752 _OnChangedVtxOffset();
753 }
754
755 ImDrawCmd *draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
756 draw_cmd->ElemCount += idx_count;
757
758 int vtx_buffer_old_size = VtxBuffer.Size;
759 VtxBuffer.resize(vtx_buffer_old_size + vtx_count);
760 _VtxWritePtr = VtxBuffer.Data + vtx_buffer_old_size;
761
762 int idx_buffer_old_size = IdxBuffer.Size;
763 IdxBuffer.resize(idx_buffer_old_size + idx_count);
764 _IdxWritePtr = IdxBuffer.Data + idx_buffer_old_size;
765}
766
767// Release the number of reserved vertices/indices from the end of the last reservation made with PrimReserve().
768void ImDrawList::PrimUnreserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
769{
770 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
771
772 ImDrawCmd *draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
773 draw_cmd->ElemCount -= idx_count;
774 VtxBuffer.shrink(VtxBuffer.Size - vtx_count);
775 IdxBuffer.shrink(IdxBuffer.Size - idx_count);
776}
777
778// Fully unrolled with inline call to keep our debug builds decently fast.
779void ImDrawList::PrimRect(const ImVec2 &a, const ImVec2 &c, ImU32 col)
780{
781 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv(_Data->TexUvWhitePixel);
782 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
783 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx;
784 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 1);
785 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
786 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx;
787 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
788 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 3);
789 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a;
790 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv;
791 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
792 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b;
793 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv;
794 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
795 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c;
796 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv;
797 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
798 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d;
799 _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv;
800 _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
801 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
802 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
803 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
804}
805
806void ImDrawList::PrimRectUV(const ImVec2 &a, const ImVec2 &c, const ImVec2 &uv_a, const ImVec2 &uv_c, ImU32 col)
807{
808 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv_b(uv_c.x, uv_a.y), uv_d(uv_a.x, uv_c.y);
809 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
810 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx;
811 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 1);
812 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
813 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx;
814 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
815 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 3);
816 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a;
817 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a;
818 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
819 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b;
820 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b;
821 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
822 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c;
823 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c;
824 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
825 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d;
826 _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d;
827 _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
828 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
829 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
830 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
831}
832
833void ImDrawList::PrimQuadUV(const ImVec2 &a, const ImVec2 &b, const ImVec2 &c, const ImVec2 &d, const ImVec2 &uv_a,
834 const ImVec2 &uv_b, const ImVec2 &uv_c, const ImVec2 &uv_d, ImU32 col)
835{
836 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
837 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx;
838 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 1);
839 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
840 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx;
841 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 2);
842 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx + 3);
843 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a;
844 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a;
845 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
846 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b;
847 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b;
848 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
849 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c;
850 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c;
851 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
852 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d;
853 _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d;
854 _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
855 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
856 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
857 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
858}
859
860// On AddPolyline() and AddConvexPolyFilled() we intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and superfluous function calls to
861// optimize debug/non-inlined builds.
862// - Those macros expects l-values and need to be used as their own statement.
863// - Those macros are intentionally not surrounded by the 'do {} while (0)' idiom because even that translates to
864// runtime with debug compilers.
865#define IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(VX, VY) \
866 { \
867 float d2 = VX * VX + VY * VY; \
868 if (d2 > 0.0f) \
869 { \
870 float inv_len = ImRsqrt(d2); \
871 VX *= inv_len; \
872 VY *= inv_len; \
873 } \
874 } \
875 (void)0
876#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2 100.0f // 500.0f (see #4053, #3366)
877#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F(VX, VY) \
878 { \
879 float d2 = VX * VX + VY * VY; \
880 if (d2 > 0.000001f) \
881 { \
882 float inv_len2 = 1.0f / d2; \
883 if (inv_len2 > IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2) \
884 inv_len2 = IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2; \
885 VX *= inv_len2; \
886 VY *= inv_len2; \
887 } \
888 } \
889 (void)0
890
891// TODO: Thickness anti-aliased lines cap are missing their AA fringe.
892// We avoid using the ImVec2 math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
893void ImDrawList::AddPolyline(const ImVec2 *points, const int points_count, ImU32 col, ImDrawFlags flags,
894 float thickness)
895{
896 if (points_count < 2 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
897 return;
898
899 const bool closed = (flags & ImDrawFlags_Closed) != 0;
900 const ImVec2 opaque_uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
901 const int count = closed ? points_count : points_count - 1; // The number of line segments we need to draw
902 const bool thick_line = (thickness > _FringeScale);
903
904 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
905 {
906 // Anti-aliased stroke
907 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
908 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
909
910 // Thicknesses <1.0 should behave like thickness 1.0
911 thickness = ImMax(thickness, 1.0f);
912 const int integer_thickness = (int)thickness;
913 const float fractional_thickness = thickness - integer_thickness;
914
915 // Do we want to draw this line using a texture?
916 // - For now, only draw integer-width lines using textures to avoid issues with the way scaling occurs, could be
917 // improved.
918 // - If AA_SIZE is not 1.0f we cannot use the texture path.
919 const bool use_texture = (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex) &&
920 (integer_thickness < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX) &&
921 (fractional_thickness <= 0.00001f) && (AA_SIZE == 1.0f);
922
923 // We should never hit this, because NewFrame() doesn't set ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex unless
924 // ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines is off
925 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(!use_texture || !(_Data->Font->ContainerAtlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines));
926
927 const int idx_count = use_texture ? (count * 6) : (thick_line ? count * 18 : count * 12);
928 const int vtx_count = use_texture ? (points_count * 2) : (thick_line ? points_count * 4 : points_count * 3);
929 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
930
931 // Temporary buffer
932 // The first <points_count> items are normals at each line point, then after that there are either 2 or 4 temp
933 // points for each line point
934 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count * ((use_texture || !thick_line) ? 3 : 5));
935 ImVec2 *temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
936 ImVec2 *temp_points = temp_normals + points_count;
937
938 // Calculate normals (tangents) for each line segment
939 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
940 {
941 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
942 float dx = points[i2].x - points[i1].x;
943 float dy = points[i2].y - points[i1].y;
944 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
945 temp_normals[i1].x = dy;
946 temp_normals[i1].y = -dx;
947 }
948 if (!closed)
949 temp_normals[points_count - 1] = temp_normals[points_count - 2];
950
951 // If we are drawing a one-pixel-wide line without a texture, or a textured line of any width, we only need 2 or
952 // 3 vertices per point
953 if (use_texture || !thick_line)
954 {
955 // [PATH 1] Texture-based lines (thick or non-thick)
956 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (non-thick)
957
958 // The width of the geometry we need to draw - this is essentially <thickness> pixels for the line itself,
959 // plus "one pixel" for AA.
960 // - In the texture-based path, we don't use AA_SIZE here because the +1 is tied to the generated texture
961 // (see ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData() function), and so alternate values won't work without changes
962 // to that code.
963 // - In the non texture-based paths, we would allow AA_SIZE to potentially be != 1.0f with a patch (e.g.
964 // fringe_scale patch to
965 // allow scaling geometry while preserving one-screen-pixel AA fringe).
966 const float half_draw_size = use_texture ? ((thickness * 0.5f) + 1) : AA_SIZE;
967
968 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals
969 // to blend
970 if (!closed)
971 {
972 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
973 temp_points[1] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
974 temp_points[(points_count - 1) * 2 + 0] =
975 points[points_count - 1] + temp_normals[points_count - 1] * half_draw_size;
976 temp_points[(points_count - 1) * 2 + 1] =
977 points[points_count - 1] - temp_normals[points_count - 1] * half_draw_size;
978 }
979
980 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line
981 // edges This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being
982 // generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
983 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
984 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
985 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
986 {
987 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1; // i2 is the second point of the line segment
988 const unsigned int idx2 = ((i1 + 1) == points_count)
989 ? _VtxCurrentIdx
990 : (idx1 + (use_texture ? 2 : 3)); // Vertex index for end of segment
991
992 // Average normals
993 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
994 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
995 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
996 dm_x *= half_draw_size; // dm_x, dm_y are offset to the outer edge of the AA area
997 dm_y *= half_draw_size;
998
999 // Add temporary vertices for the outer edges
1000 ImVec2 *out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 2];
1001 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_x;
1002 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_y;
1003 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x - dm_x;
1004 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y - dm_y;
1005
1006 if (use_texture)
1007 {
1008 // Add indices for two triangles
1009 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0);
1010 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
1011 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); // Right tri
1012 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1013 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1);
1014 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Left tri
1015 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1016 }
1017 else
1018 {
1019 // Add indexes for four triangles
1020 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0);
1021 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
1022 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); // Right tri 1
1023 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
1024 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
1025 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Right tri 2
1026 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1027 _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1);
1028 _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); // Left tri 1
1029 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
1030 _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0);
1031 _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); // Left tri 2
1032 _IdxWritePtr += 12;
1033 }
1034
1035 idx1 = idx2;
1036 }
1037
1038 // Add vertices for each point on the line
1039 if (use_texture)
1040 {
1041 // If we're using textures we only need to emit the left/right edge vertices
1042 ImVec4 tex_uvs = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness];
1043 /*if (fractional_thickness != 0.0f) // Currently always zero when use_texture==false!
1044 {
1045 const ImVec4 tex_uvs_1 = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness + 1];
1046 tex_uvs.x = tex_uvs.x + (tex_uvs_1.x - tex_uvs.x) * fractional_thickness; // inlined ImLerp()
1047 tex_uvs.y = tex_uvs.y + (tex_uvs_1.y - tex_uvs.y) * fractional_thickness;
1048 tex_uvs.z = tex_uvs.z + (tex_uvs_1.z - tex_uvs.z) * fractional_thickness;
1049 tex_uvs.w = tex_uvs.w + (tex_uvs_1.w - tex_uvs.w) * fractional_thickness;
1050 }*/
1051 ImVec2 tex_uv0(tex_uvs.x, tex_uvs.y);
1052 ImVec2 tex_uv1(tex_uvs.z, tex_uvs.w);
1053 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
1054 {
1055 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0];
1056 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = tex_uv0;
1057 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Left-side outer edge
1058 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1];
1059 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = tex_uv1;
1060 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col; // Right-side outer edge
1061 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1062 }
1063 }
1064 else
1065 {
1066 // If we're not using a texture, we need the center vertex as well
1067 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
1068 {
1069 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i];
1070 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv;
1071 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Center of line
1072 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0];
1073 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv;
1074 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Left-side outer edge
1075 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1];
1076 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv;
1077 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col_trans; // Right-side outer edge
1078 _VtxWritePtr += 3;
1079 }
1080 }
1081 }
1082 else
1083 {
1084 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (thick): we need to draw the solid line core and thus require four
1085 // vertices per point
1086 const float half_inner_thickness = (thickness - AA_SIZE) * 0.5f;
1087
1088 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals
1089 // to blend
1090 if (!closed)
1091 {
1092 const int points_last = points_count - 1;
1093 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1094 temp_points[1] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
1095 temp_points[2] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
1096 temp_points[3] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1097 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 0] =
1098 points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1099 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 1] =
1100 points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
1101 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 2] =
1102 points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
1103 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 3] =
1104 points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1105 }
1106
1107 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line
1108 // edges This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being
1109 // generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
1110 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
1111 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
1112 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
1113 {
1114 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : (i1 + 1); // i2 is the second point of the line segment
1115 const unsigned int idx2 =
1116 (i1 + 1) == points_count ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + 4); // Vertex index for end of segment
1117
1118 // Average normals
1119 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
1120 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
1121 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1122 float dm_out_x = dm_x * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1123 float dm_out_y = dm_y * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
1124 float dm_in_x = dm_x * half_inner_thickness;
1125 float dm_in_y = dm_y * half_inner_thickness;
1126
1127 // Add temporary vertices
1128 ImVec2 *out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 4];
1129 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_out_x;
1130 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_out_y;
1131 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x + dm_in_x;
1132 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y + dm_in_y;
1133 out_vtx[2].x = points[i2].x - dm_in_x;
1134 out_vtx[2].y = points[i2].y - dm_in_y;
1135 out_vtx[3].x = points[i2].x - dm_out_x;
1136 out_vtx[3].y = points[i2].y - dm_out_y;
1137
1138 // Add indexes
1139 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1140 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1);
1141 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
1142 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
1143 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
1144 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1145 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1146 _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1);
1147 _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
1148 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
1149 _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0);
1150 _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
1151 _IdxWritePtr[12] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
1152 _IdxWritePtr[13] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
1153 _IdxWritePtr[14] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3);
1154 _IdxWritePtr[15] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3);
1155 _IdxWritePtr[16] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 3);
1156 _IdxWritePtr[17] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
1157 _IdxWritePtr += 18;
1158
1159 idx1 = idx2;
1160 }
1161
1162 // Add vertices
1163 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
1164 {
1165 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 0];
1166 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv;
1167 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col_trans;
1168 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 1];
1169 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv;
1170 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
1171 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 2];
1172 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv;
1173 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
1174 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 3];
1175 _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv;
1176 _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col_trans;
1177 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
1178 }
1179 }
1180 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1181 }
1182 else
1183 {
1184 // [PATH 4] Non texture-based, Non anti-aliased lines
1185 const int idx_count = count * 6;
1186 const int vtx_count = count * 4; // FIXME-OPT: Not sharing edges
1187 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1188
1189 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
1190 {
1191 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
1192 const ImVec2 &p1 = points[i1];
1193 const ImVec2 &p2 = points[i2];
1194
1195 float dx = p2.x - p1.x;
1196 float dy = p2.y - p1.y;
1197 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1198 dx *= (thickness * 0.5f);
1199 dy *= (thickness * 0.5f);
1200
1201 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = p1.x + dy;
1202 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = p1.y - dx;
1203 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv;
1204 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1205 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = p2.x + dy;
1206 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = p2.y - dx;
1207 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv;
1208 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
1209 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.x = p2.x - dy;
1210 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.y = p2.y + dx;
1211 _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv;
1212 _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
1213 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.x = p1.x - dy;
1214 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.y = p1.y + dx;
1215 _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv;
1216 _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
1217 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
1218
1219 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx);
1220 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1);
1221 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2);
1222 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx);
1223 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2);
1224 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3);
1225 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1226 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
1227 }
1228 }
1229}
1230
1231// - We intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and its math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined
1232// builds.
1233// - Filled shapes must always use clockwise winding order. The anti-aliasing fringe depends on it. Counter-clockwise
1234// shapes will have "inward" anti-aliasing.
1235void ImDrawList::AddConvexPolyFilled(const ImVec2 *points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
1236{
1237 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1238 return;
1239
1240 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1241
1242 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
1243 {
1244 // Anti-aliased Fill
1245 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
1246 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
1247 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3 + points_count * 6;
1248 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
1249 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1250
1251 // Add indexes for fill
1252 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
1253 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
1254 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1255 {
1256 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx);
1257 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + ((i - 1) << 1));
1258 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i << 1));
1259 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1260 }
1261
1262 // Compute normals
1263 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
1264 ImVec2 *temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
1265 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1266 {
1267 const ImVec2 &p0 = points[i0];
1268 const ImVec2 &p1 = points[i1];
1269 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
1270 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
1271 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1272 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
1273 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
1274 }
1275
1276 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1277 {
1278 // Average normals
1279 const ImVec2 &n0 = temp_normals[i0];
1280 const ImVec2 &n1 = temp_normals[i1];
1281 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
1282 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
1283 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1284 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1285 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1286
1287 // Add vertices
1288 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x);
1289 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y);
1290 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv;
1291 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
1292 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x);
1293 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y);
1294 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv;
1295 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
1296 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1297
1298 // Add indexes for fringes
1299 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1300 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1));
1301 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1302 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1303 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1));
1304 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1305 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1306 }
1307 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1308 }
1309 else
1310 {
1311 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
1312 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3;
1313 const int vtx_count = points_count;
1314 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1315 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
1316 {
1317 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i];
1318 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv;
1319 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1320 _VtxWritePtr++;
1321 }
1322 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1323 {
1324 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx);
1325 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i - 1);
1326 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i);
1327 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1328 }
1329 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1330 }
1331}
1332
1333void ImDrawList::_PathArcToFastEx(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, int a_min_sample, int a_max_sample, int a_step)
1334{
1335 if (radius < 0.5f)
1336 {
1337 _Path.push_back(center);
1338 return;
1339 }
1340
1341 // Calculate arc auto segment step size
1342 if (a_step <= 0)
1343 a_step = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1344
1345 // Make sure we never do steps larger than one quarter of the circle
1346 a_step = ImClamp(a_step, 1, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_TABLE_SIZE / 4);
1347
1348 const int sample_range = ImAbs(a_max_sample - a_min_sample);
1349 const int a_next_step = a_step;
1350
1351 int samples = sample_range + 1;
1352 bool extra_max_sample = false;
1353 if (a_step > 1)
1354 {
1355 samples = sample_range / a_step + 1;
1356 const int overstep = sample_range % a_step;
1357
1358 if (overstep > 0)
1359 {
1360 extra_max_sample = true;
1361 samples++;
1362
1363 // When we have overstep to avoid awkwardly looking one long line and one tiny one at the end,
1364 // distribute first step range evenly between them by reducing first step size.
1365 if (sample_range > 0)
1366 a_step -= (a_step - overstep) / 2;
1367 }
1368 }
1369
1370 _Path.resize(_Path.Size + samples);
1371 ImVec2 *out_ptr = _Path.Data + (_Path.Size - samples);
1372
1373 int sample_index = a_min_sample;
1374 if (sample_index < 0 || sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1375 {
1376 sample_index = sample_index % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1377 if (sample_index < 0)
1378 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1379 }
1380
1381 if (a_max_sample >= a_min_sample)
1382 {
1383 for (int a = a_min_sample; a <= a_max_sample; a += a_step, sample_index += a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1384 {
1385 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over
1386 // range twice or more
1387 if (sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1388 sample_index -= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1389
1390 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1391 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1392 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1393 out_ptr++;
1394 }
1395 }
1396 else
1397 {
1398 for (int a = a_min_sample; a >= a_max_sample; a -= a_step, sample_index -= a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1399 {
1400 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over
1401 // range twice or more
1402 if (sample_index < 0)
1403 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1404
1405 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1406 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1407 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1408 out_ptr++;
1409 }
1410 }
1411
1412 if (extra_max_sample)
1413 {
1414 int normalized_max_sample = a_max_sample % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1415 if (normalized_max_sample < 0)
1416 normalized_max_sample += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1417
1418 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[normalized_max_sample];
1419 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1420 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1421 out_ptr++;
1422 }
1423
1424 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(_Path.Data + _Path.Size == out_ptr);
1425}
1426
1427void ImDrawList::_PathArcToN(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1428{
1429 if (radius < 0.5f)
1430 {
1431 _Path.push_back(center);
1432 return;
1433 }
1434
1435 // Note that we are adding a point at both a_min and a_max.
1436 // If you are trying to draw a full closed circle you don't want the overlapping points!
1437 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1438 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1439 {
1440 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1441 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a) * radius));
1442 }
1443}
1444
1445// 0: East, 3: South, 6: West, 9: North, 12: East
1446void ImDrawList::PathArcToFast(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, int a_min_of_12, int a_max_of_12)
1447{
1448 if (radius < 0.5f)
1449 {
1450 _Path.push_back(center);
1451 return;
1452 }
1453 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12,
1454 a_max_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, 0);
1455}
1456
1457void ImDrawList::PathArcTo(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1458{
1459 if (radius < 0.5f)
1460 {
1461 _Path.push_back(center);
1462 return;
1463 }
1464
1465 if (num_segments > 0)
1466 {
1467 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, num_segments);
1468 return;
1469 }
1470
1471 // Automatic segment count
1472 if (radius <= _Data->ArcFastRadiusCutoff)
1473 {
1474 const bool a_is_reverse = a_max < a_min;
1475
1476 // We are going to use precomputed values for mid samples.
1477 // Determine first and last sample in lookup table that belong to the arc.
1478 const float a_min_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_min / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1479 const float a_max_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_max / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1480
1481 const int a_min_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImFloor(a_min_sample_f) : (int)ImCeil(a_min_sample_f);
1482 const int a_max_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImCeil(a_max_sample_f) : (int)ImFloor(a_max_sample_f);
1483 const int a_mid_samples =
1484 a_is_reverse ? ImMax(a_min_sample - a_max_sample, 0) : ImMax(a_max_sample - a_min_sample, 0);
1485
1486 const float a_min_segment_angle = a_min_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1487 const float a_max_segment_angle = a_max_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1488 const bool a_emit_start = ImAbs(a_min_segment_angle - a_min) >= 1e-5f;
1489 const bool a_emit_end = ImAbs(a_max - a_max_segment_angle) >= 1e-5f;
1490
1491 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (a_mid_samples + 1 + (a_emit_start ? 1 : 0) + (a_emit_end ? 1 : 0)));
1492 if (a_emit_start)
1493 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_min) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_min) * radius));
1494 if (a_mid_samples > 0)
1495 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_sample, a_max_sample, 0);
1496 if (a_emit_end)
1497 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_max) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_max) * radius));
1498 }
1499 else
1500 {
1501 const float arc_length = ImAbs(a_max - a_min);
1502 const int circle_segment_count = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1503 const int arc_segment_count =
1504 ImMax((int)ImCeil(circle_segment_count * arc_length / (IM_PI * 2.0f)), (int)(2.0f * IM_PI / arc_length));
1505 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, arc_segment_count);
1506 }
1507}
1508
1509void ImDrawList::PathEllipticalArcTo(const ImVec2 &center, const ImVec2 &radius, float rot, float a_min, float a_max,
1510 int num_segments)
1511{
1512 if (num_segments <= 0)
1513 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(
1514 ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1515
1516 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1517
1518 const float cos_rot = ImCos(rot);
1519 const float sin_rot = ImSin(rot);
1520 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1521 {
1522 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1523 ImVec2 point(ImCos(a) * radius.x, ImSin(a) * radius.y);
1524 const ImVec2 rel((point.x * cos_rot) - (point.y * sin_rot), (point.x * sin_rot) + (point.y * cos_rot));
1525 point.x = rel.x + center.x;
1526 point.y = rel.y + center.y;
1527 _Path.push_back(point);
1528 }
1529}
1530
1531ImVec2 ImBezierCubicCalc(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, const ImVec2 &p4, float t)
1532{
1533 float u = 1.0f - t;
1534 float w1 = u * u * u;
1535 float w2 = 3 * u * u * t;
1536 float w3 = 3 * u * t * t;
1537 float w4 = t * t * t;
1538 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x + w4 * p4.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y + w4 * p4.y);
1539}
1540
1541ImVec2 ImBezierQuadraticCalc(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, float t)
1542{
1543 float u = 1.0f - t;
1544 float w1 = u * u;
1545 float w2 = 2 * u * t;
1546 float w3 = t * t;
1547 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y);
1548}
1549
1550// Closely mimics ImBezierCubicClosestPointCasteljau() in imgui.cpp
1551static void PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2> *path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3,
1552 float y3, float x4, float y4, float tess_tol, int level)
1553{
1554 float dx = x4 - x1;
1555 float dy = y4 - y1;
1556 float d2 = (x2 - x4) * dy - (y2 - y4) * dx;
1557 float d3 = (x3 - x4) * dy - (y3 - y4) * dx;
1558 d2 = (d2 >= 0) ? d2 : -d2;
1559 d3 = (d3 >= 0) ? d3 : -d3;
1560 if ((d2 + d3) * (d2 + d3) < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1561 {
1562 path->push_back(ImVec2(x4, y4));
1563 }
1564 else if (level < 10)
1565 {
1566 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1567 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1568 float x34 = (x3 + x4) * 0.5f, y34 = (y3 + y4) * 0.5f;
1569 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1570 float x234 = (x23 + x34) * 0.5f, y234 = (y23 + y34) * 0.5f;
1571 float x1234 = (x123 + x234) * 0.5f, y1234 = (y123 + y234) * 0.5f;
1572 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, x1234, y1234, tess_tol, level + 1);
1573 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1234, y1234, x234, y234, x34, y34, x4, y4, tess_tol, level + 1);
1574 }
1575}
1576
1577static void PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2> *path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2,
1578 float x3, float y3, float tess_tol, int level)
1579{
1580 float dx = x3 - x1, dy = y3 - y1;
1581 float det = (x2 - x3) * dy - (y2 - y3) * dx;
1582 if (det * det * 4.0f < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1583 {
1584 path->push_back(ImVec2(x3, y3));
1585 }
1586 else if (level < 10)
1587 {
1588 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1589 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1590 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1591 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, tess_tol, level + 1);
1592 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x123, y123, x23, y23, x3, y3, tess_tol, level + 1);
1593 }
1594}
1595
1596void ImDrawList::PathBezierCubicCurveTo(const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, const ImVec2 &p4, int num_segments)
1597{
1598 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1599 if (num_segments == 0)
1600 {
1601 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1602 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, p4.x, p4.y,
1603 _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0); // Auto-tessellated
1604 }
1605 else
1606 {
1607 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1608 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1609 _Path.push_back(ImBezierCubicCalc(p1, p2, p3, p4, t_step * i_step));
1610 }
1611}
1612
1613void ImDrawList::PathBezierQuadraticCurveTo(const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, int num_segments)
1614{
1615 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1616 if (num_segments == 0)
1617 {
1618 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1619 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol,
1620 0); // Auto-tessellated
1621 }
1622 else
1623 {
1624 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1625 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1626 _Path.push_back(ImBezierQuadraticCalc(p1, p2, p3, t_step * i_step));
1627 }
1628}
1629
1630static inline ImDrawFlags FixRectCornerFlags(ImDrawFlags flags)
1631{
1632 /*
1633 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft == (1 << 4));
1634#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_OBSOLETE_FUNCTIONS
1635 // Obsoleted in 1.82 (from February 2021). This code was stripped/simplified and mostly commented in 1.90 (from
1636September 2023)
1637 // - Legacy Support for hard coded ~0 (used to be a suggested equivalent to ImDrawCornerFlags_All)
1638 if (flags == ~0) { return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll; }
1639 // - Legacy Support for hard coded 0x01 to 0x0F (matching 15 out of 16 old flags combinations). Read details in
1640older version of this code. if (flags >= 0x01 && flags <= 0x0F) { return (flags << 4); }
1641 // We cannot support hard coded 0x00 with 'float rounding > 0.0f' --> replace with ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone or
1642use 'float rounding = 0.0f' #endif
1643 */
1644 // If this assert triggers, please update your code replacing hardcoded values with new ImDrawFlags_RoundCorners*
1645 // values. Note that ImDrawFlags_Closed (== 0x01) is an invalid flag for AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect() etc.
1646 // anyway. See details in 1.82 Changelog as well as 2021/03/12 and 2023/09/08 entries in "API BREAKING CHANGES"
1647 // section.
1648 IM_ASSERT((flags & 0x0F) == 0 && "Misuse of legacy hardcoded ImDrawCornerFlags values!");
1649
1650 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
1651 flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll;
1652
1653 return flags;
1654}
1655
1656void ImDrawList::PathRect(const ImVec2 &a, const ImVec2 &b, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1657{
1658 if (rounding >= 0.5f)
1659 {
1660 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1661 rounding = ImMin(rounding,
1662 ImFabs(b.x - a.x) *
1663 (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) ||
1664 ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom)
1665 ? 0.5f
1666 : 1.0f) -
1667 1.0f);
1668 rounding =
1669 ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.y - a.y) *
1670 (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) ||
1671 ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight)
1672 ? 0.5f
1673 : 1.0f) -
1674 1.0f);
1675 }
1676 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1677 {
1678 PathLineTo(a);
1679 PathLineTo(ImVec2(b.x, a.y));
1680 PathLineTo(b);
1681 PathLineTo(ImVec2(a.x, b.y));
1682 }
1683 else
1684 {
1685 const float rounding_tl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1686 const float rounding_tr = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1687 const float rounding_br = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1688 const float rounding_bl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1689 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_tl, a.y + rounding_tl), rounding_tl, 6, 9);
1690 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_tr, a.y + rounding_tr), rounding_tr, 9, 12);
1691 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_br, b.y - rounding_br), rounding_br, 0, 3);
1692 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_bl, b.y - rounding_bl), rounding_bl, 3, 6);
1693 }
1694}
1695
1696void ImDrawList::AddLine(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, ImU32 col, float thickness)
1697{
1698 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1699 return;
1700 PathLineTo(p1 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1701 PathLineTo(p2 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1702 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1703}
1704
1705// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1706// Note we don't render 1 pixels sized rectangles properly.
1707void ImDrawList::AddRect(const ImVec2 &p_min, const ImVec2 &p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags,
1708 float thickness)
1709{
1710 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1711 return;
1712 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
1713 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), rounding, flags);
1714 else
1715 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.49f, 0.49f), rounding,
1716 flags); // Better looking lower-right corner and rounded non-AA shapes.
1717 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1718}
1719
1720void ImDrawList::AddRectFilled(const ImVec2 &p_min, const ImVec2 &p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1721{
1722 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1723 return;
1724 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1725 {
1726 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1727 PrimRect(p_min, p_max, col);
1728 }
1729 else
1730 {
1731 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1732 PathFillConvex(col);
1733 }
1734}
1735
1736// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1737void ImDrawList::AddRectFilledMultiColor(const ImVec2 &p_min, const ImVec2 &p_max, ImU32 col_upr_left,
1738 ImU32 col_upr_right, ImU32 col_bot_right, ImU32 col_bot_left)
1739{
1740 if (((col_upr_left | col_upr_right | col_bot_right | col_bot_left) & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1741 return;
1742
1743 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1744 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1745 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx));
1746 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1));
1747 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2));
1748 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx));
1749 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2));
1750 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3));
1751 PrimWriteVtx(p_min, uv, col_upr_left);
1752 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_max.x, p_min.y), uv, col_upr_right);
1753 PrimWriteVtx(p_max, uv, col_bot_right);
1754 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_min.x, p_max.y), uv, col_bot_left);
1755}

1768}

1770void ImDrawList::AddQuadFilled(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, const ImVec2 &p4, ImU32 col)

1782void ImDrawList::AddTriangle(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, ImU32 col, float thickness)

1792
1793void ImDrawList::AddTriangleFilled(const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3, ImU32 col)
1794{
1795 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1796 return;
1797
1798 PathLineTo(p1);
1799 PathLineTo(p2);
1800 PathLineTo(p3);
1801 PathFillConvex(col);
1802}
1803
1804void ImDrawList::AddCircle(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1805{
1806 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1807 return;
1808
1809 if (num_segments <= 0)
1810 {
1811 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1812 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius - 0.5f, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1813 _Path.Size--;
1814 }
1815 else
1816 {
1817 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1818 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1819
1820 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1821 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1822 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1823 }
1824
1825 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1826}
1827
1828void ImDrawList::AddCircleFilled(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1829{
1830 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1831 return;
1832
1833 if (num_segments <= 0)
1834 {
1835 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1836 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1837 _Path.Size--;
1838 }
1839 else
1840 {
1841 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1842 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1843
1844 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1845 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1846 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1847 }
1848
1849 PathFillConvex(col);
1850}
1851
1852// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1853void ImDrawList::AddNgon(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1854{
1855 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1856 return;
1857
1858 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1859 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1860 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1861 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1862}
1863
1864// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1865void ImDrawList::AddNgonFilled(const ImVec2 &center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1866{
1867 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1868 return;
1869
1870 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1871 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1872 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1873 PathFillConvex(col);
1874}
1875
1876// Ellipse
1877void ImDrawList::AddEllipse(const ImVec2 &center, const ImVec2 &radius, ImU32 col, float rot, int num_segments,
1878 float thickness)
1879{
1880 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1881 return;
1882
1883 if (num_segments <= 0)
1884 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(
1885 ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1886
1887 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1888 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1889 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1890 PathStroke(col, true, thickness);
1891}
1892
1893void ImDrawList::AddEllipseFilled(const ImVec2 &center, const ImVec2 &radius, ImU32 col, float rot, int num_segments)
1894{
1895 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1896 return;
1897
1898 if (num_segments <= 0)
1899 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(
1900 ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1901
1902 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1903 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1904 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1905 PathFillConvex(col);
1906}

1932void ImDrawList::AddText(ImFont *font, float font_size, const ImVec2 &pos, ImU32 col, const char *text_begin,
1933 const char *text_end, float wrap_width, const ImVec4 *cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1934{
1935 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1936 return;
1937
1938 // Accept null ranges
1939 if (text_begin == text_end || text_begin[0] == 0)
1940 return;
1941 // No need to strlen() here: font->RenderText() will do it and may early out.
1942
1943 // Pull default font/size from the shared ImDrawListSharedData instance
1944 if (font == NULL)
1945 font = _Data->Font;
1946 if (font_size == 0.0f)
1947 font_size = _Data->FontSize;
1948
1949 IM_ASSERT(font->ContainerAtlas->TexID == _CmdHeader.TextureId); // Use high-level ImGui::PushFont() or low-level
1950 // ImDrawList::PushTextureId() to change font.
1951
1952 ImVec4 clip_rect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
1953 if (cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1954 {
1955 clip_rect.x = ImMax(clip_rect.x, cpu_fine_clip_rect->x);
1956 clip_rect.y = ImMax(clip_rect.y, cpu_fine_clip_rect->y);
1957 clip_rect.z = ImMin(clip_rect.z, cpu_fine_clip_rect->z);
1958 clip_rect.w = ImMin(clip_rect.w, cpu_fine_clip_rect->w);
1959 }
1960 font->RenderText(this, font_size, pos, col, clip_rect, text_begin, text_end, wrap_width,
1961 cpu_fine_clip_rect != NULL);
1962}
1963
1964void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImVec2 &pos, ImU32 col, const char *text_begin, const char *text_end)
1965{
1966 AddText(_Data->Font, _Data->FontSize, pos, col, text_begin, text_end);
1967}
