1969void ImDrawList::AddImage(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2 &p_min, const ImVec2 &p_max, const ImVec2 &uv_min,
1970 const ImVec2 &uv_max, ImU32 col)
1971{
1972 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1973 return;
1974
1975 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1976 if (push_texture_id)
1977 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1978
1979 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1980 PrimRectUV(p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1981
1982 if (push_texture_id)
1983 PopTextureID();
1984}
1985
1986void ImDrawList::AddImageQuad(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2 &p1, const ImVec2 &p2, const ImVec2 &p3,
1987 const ImVec2 &p4, const ImVec2 &uv1, const ImVec2 &uv2, const ImVec2 &uv3,
1988 const ImVec2 &uv4, ImU32 col)
1989{
1990 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1991 return;
1992
1993 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1994 if (push_texture_id)
1995 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1996
1997 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1998 PrimQuadUV(p1, p2, p3, p4, uv1, uv2, uv3, uv4, col);
1999
2000 if (push_texture_id)
2001 PopTextureID();
2002}
2003
2004void ImDrawList::AddImageRounded(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2 &p_min, const ImVec2 &p_max,
2005 const ImVec2 &uv_min, const ImVec2 &uv_max, ImU32 col, float rounding,
2006 ImDrawFlags flags)
2007{
2008 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
2009 return;
2010
2011 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
2012 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
2013 {
2014 AddImage(user_texture_id, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
2015 return;
2016 }
2017
2018 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
2019 if (push_texture_id)
2020 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
2021
2022 int vert_start_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
2023 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
2024 PathFillConvex(col);
2025 int vert_end_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
2026 ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(this, vert_start_idx, vert_end_idx, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, true);
2027
2028 if (push_texture_id)
2029 PopTextureID();
2030}
2031
2032//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2033// [SECTION] ImTriangulator, ImDrawList concave polygon fill
2034//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2035// Triangulate concave polygons. Based on "Triangulation by Ear Clipping" paper, O(N^2) complexity.
2036// Reference: https://www.geometrictools.com/Documentation/TriangulationByEarClipping.pdf
2037// Provided as a convenience for user but not used by main library.
2038//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2039// - ImTriangulator [Internal]
2040// - AddConcavePolyFilled()
2041//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2042
2043enum ImTriangulatorNodeType
2044{
2045 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex,
2046 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear,
2047 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex
2048};
2049
2050struct ImTriangulatorNode
2051{
2052 ImTriangulatorNodeType Type;
2053 int Index;
2054 ImVec2 Pos;
2055 ImTriangulatorNode *Next;
2056 ImTriangulatorNode *Prev;
2057
2058 void Unlink()
2059 {
2060 Next->Prev = Prev;
2061 Prev->Next = Next;
2062 }
2063};
2064
2065struct ImTriangulatorNodeSpan
2066{
2067 ImTriangulatorNode **Data = NULL;
2068 int Size = 0;
2069
2070 void push_back(ImTriangulatorNode *node)
2071 {
2072 Data[Size++] = node;
2073 }
2074 void find_erase_unsorted(int idx)
2075 {
2076 for (int i = Size - 1; i >= 0; i--)
2077 if (Data[i]->Index == idx)
2078 {
2079 Data[i] = Data[Size - 1];
2080 Size--;
2081 return;
2082 }
2083 }
2084};
2085
2086struct ImTriangulator
2087{
2088 static int EstimateTriangleCount(int points_count)
2089 {
2090 return (points_count < 3) ? 0 : points_count - 2;
2091 }
2092 static int EstimateScratchBufferSize(int points_count)
2093 {
2094 return sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode) * points_count + sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode *) * points_count * 2;
2095 }
2096
2097 void Init(const ImVec2 *points, int points_count, void *scratch_buffer);
2098 void GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3]); // Return relative indexes for next triangle
2099
2100 // Internal functions
2101 void BuildNodes(const ImVec2 *points, int points_count);
2102 void BuildReflexes();
2103 void BuildEars();
2104 void FlipNodeList();
2105 bool IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2 &v0, const ImVec2 &v1, const ImVec2 &v2) const;
2106 void ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode *node);
2107
2108 // Internal members
2109 int _TrianglesLeft = 0;
2110 ImTriangulatorNode *_Nodes = NULL;
2111 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Ears;
2112 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Reflexes;
2113};
2114
2115// Distribute storage for nodes, ears and reflexes.
2116// FIXME-OPT: if everything is convex, we could report it to caller and let it switch to an convex renderer
2117// (this would require first building reflexes to bail to convex if empty, without even building nodes)
2118void ImTriangulator::Init(const ImVec2 *points, int points_count, void *scratch_buffer)
2119{
2120 IM_ASSERT(scratch_buffer != NULL && points_count >= 3);
2121 _TrianglesLeft = EstimateTriangleCount(points_count);
2122 _Nodes = (ImTriangulatorNode *)scratch_buffer; // points_count x Node
2123 _Ears.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode **)(_Nodes + points_count); // points_count x Node*
2124 _Reflexes.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode **)(_Nodes + points_count) + points_count; // points_count x Node*
2125 BuildNodes(points, points_count);
2126 BuildReflexes();
2127 BuildEars();
2128}
2129
2130void ImTriangulator::BuildNodes(const ImVec2 *points, int points_count)
2131{
2132 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
2133 {
2134 _Nodes[i].Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
2135 _Nodes[i].Index = i;
2136 _Nodes[i].Pos = points[i];
2137 _Nodes[i].Next = _Nodes + i + 1;
2138 _Nodes[i].Prev = _Nodes + i - 1;
2139 }
2140 _Nodes[0].Prev = _Nodes + points_count - 1;
2141 _Nodes[points_count - 1].Next = _Nodes;
2142}
2143
2144void ImTriangulator::BuildReflexes()
2145{
2146 ImTriangulatorNode *n1 = _Nodes;
2147 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
2148 {
2149 if (ImTriangleIsClockwise(n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
2150 continue;
2151 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
2152 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
2153 }
2154}
2155
2156void ImTriangulator::BuildEars()
2157{
2158 ImTriangulatorNode *n1 = _Nodes;
2159 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
2160 {
2161 if (n1->Type != ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex)
2162 continue;
2163 if (!IsEar(n1->Prev->Index, n1->Index, n1->Next->Index, n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
2164 continue;
2165 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
2166 _Ears.push_back(n1);
2167 }
2168}
2169
2170void ImTriangulator::GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3])
2171{
2172 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
2173 {
2174 FlipNodeList();
2175
2176 ImTriangulatorNode *node = _Nodes;
2177 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, node = node->Next)
2178 node->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
2179 _Reflexes.Size = 0;
2180 BuildReflexes();
2181 BuildEars();
2182
2183 // If we still don't have ears, it means geometry is degenerated.
2184 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
2185 {
2186 // Return first triangle available, mimicking the behavior of convex fill.
2187 IM_ASSERT(_TrianglesLeft > 0); // Geometry is degenerated
2188 _Ears.Data[0] = _Nodes;
2189 _Ears.Size = 1;
2190 }
2191 }
2192
2193 ImTriangulatorNode *ear = _Ears.Data[--_Ears.Size];
2194 out_triangle[0] = ear->Prev->Index;
2195 out_triangle[1] = ear->Index;
2196 out_triangle[2] = ear->Next->Index;
2197
2198 ear->Unlink();
2199 if (ear == _Nodes)
2200 _Nodes = ear->Next;
2201
2202 ReclassifyNode(ear->Prev);
2203 ReclassifyNode(ear->Next);
2204 _TrianglesLeft--;
2205}
2206
2207void ImTriangulator::FlipNodeList()
2208{
2209 ImTriangulatorNode *prev = _Nodes;
2210 ImTriangulatorNode *temp = _Nodes;
2211 ImTriangulatorNode *current = _Nodes->Next;
2212 prev->Next = prev;
2213 prev->Prev = prev;
2214 while (current != _Nodes)
2215 {
2216 temp = current->Next;
2217
2218 current->Next = prev;
2219 prev->Prev = current;
2220 _Nodes->Next = current;
2221 current->Prev = _Nodes;
2222
2223 prev = current;
2224 current = temp;
2225 }
2226 _Nodes = prev;
2227}
2228
2229// A triangle is an ear is no other vertex is inside it. We can test reflexes vertices only (see reference algorithm)
2230bool ImTriangulator::IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2 &v0, const ImVec2 &v1, const ImVec2 &v2) const
2231{
2232 ImTriangulatorNode **p_end = _Reflexes.Data + _Reflexes.Size;
2233 for (ImTriangulatorNode **p = _Reflexes.Data; p < p_end; p++)
2234 {
2235 ImTriangulatorNode *reflex = *p;
2236 if (reflex->Index != i0 && reflex->Index != i1 && reflex->Index != i2)
2237 if (ImTriangleContainsPoint(v0, v1, v2, reflex->Pos))
2238 return false;
2239 }
2240 return true;
2241}
2242
2243void ImTriangulator::ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode *n1)
2244{
2245 // Classify node
2246 ImTriangulatorNodeType type;
2247 const ImTriangulatorNode *n0 = n1->Prev;
2248 const ImTriangulatorNode *n2 = n1->Next;
2249 if (!ImTriangleIsClockwise(n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
2250 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
2251 else if (IsEar(n0->Index, n1->Index, n2->Index, n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
2252 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
2253 else
2254 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
2255
2256 // Update lists when a type changes
2257 if (type == n1->Type)
2258 return;
2259 if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
2260 _Reflexes.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
2261 else if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
2262 _Ears.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
2263 if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
2264 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
2265 else if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
2266 _Ears.push_back(n1);
2267 n1->Type = type;
2268}
2269
2270// Use ear-clipping algorithm to triangulate a simple polygon (no self-interaction, no holes).
2271// (Reminder: we don't perform any coarse clipping/culling in ImDrawList layer!
2272// It is up to caller to ensure not making costly calls that will be outside of visible area.
2273// As concave fill is noticeably more expensive than other primitives, be mindful of this...
2274// Caller can build AABB of points, and avoid filling if 'draw_list->_CmdHeader.ClipRect.Overlays(points_bb) == false')
2275void ImDrawList::AddConcavePolyFilled(const ImVec2 *points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
2276{
2277 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
2278 return;
2279
2280 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
2281 ImTriangulator triangulator;
2282 unsigned int triangle[3];
2283 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
2284 {
2285 // Anti-aliased Fill
2286 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
2287 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
2288 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3 + points_count * 6;
2289 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
2290 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
2291
2292 // Add indexes for fill
2293 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
2294 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
2295
2296 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) /
2297 sizeof(ImVec2));
2298 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
2299 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
2300 {
2301 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
2302 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[0] << 1));
2303 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[1] << 1));
2304 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[2] << 1));
2305 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
2306 }
2307
2308 // Compute normals
2309 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
2310 ImVec2 *temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
2311 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
2312 {
2313 const ImVec2 &p0 = points[i0];
2314 const ImVec2 &p1 = points[i1];
2315 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
2316 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
2317 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
2318 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
2319 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
2320 }
2321
2322 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
2323 {
2324 // Average normals
2325 const ImVec2 &n0 = temp_normals[i0];
2326 const ImVec2 &n1 = temp_normals[i1];
2327 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
2328 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
2329 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
2330 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
2331 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
2332
2333 // Add vertices
2334 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x);
2335 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y);
2336 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv;
2337 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
2338 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x);
2339 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y);
2340 _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv;
2341 _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
2342 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
2343
2344 // Add indexes for fringes
2345 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
2346 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1));
2347 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
2348 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
2349 _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1));
2350 _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
2351 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
2352 }
2353 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
2354 }
2355 else
2356 {
2357 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
2358 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3;
2359 const int vtx_count = points_count;
2360 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
2361 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
2362 {
2363 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i];
2364 _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv;
2365 _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
2366 _VtxWritePtr++;
2367 }
2368 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) /
2369 sizeof(ImVec2));
2370 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
2371 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
2372 {
2373 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
2374 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[0]);
2375 _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[1]);
2376 _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[2]);
2377 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
2378 }
2379 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
2380 }
2381}
2382
2383//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2384// [SECTION] ImDrawListSplitter
2385//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2386// FIXME: This may be a little confusing, trying to be a little too low-level/optimal instead of just doing vector
2387// swap..
2388//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2389
2390void ImDrawListSplitter::ClearFreeMemory()
2391{
2392 for (int i = 0; i < _Channels.Size; i++)
2393 {
2394 if (i == _Current)
2395 memset(&_Channels[i], 0,
2396 sizeof(_Channels[i])); // Current channel is a copy of CmdBuffer/IdxBuffer, don't destruct again
2397 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.clear();
2398 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.clear();
2399 }
2400 _Current = 0;
2401 _Count = 1;
2402 _Channels.clear();
2403}
2404
2405void ImDrawListSplitter::Split(ImDrawList *draw_list, int channels_count)
2406{
2407 IM_UNUSED(draw_list);
2408 IM_ASSERT(_Current == 0 && _Count <= 1 &&
2409 "Nested channel splitting is not supported. Please use separate instances of ImDrawListSplitter.");
2410 int old_channels_count = _Channels.Size;
2411 if (old_channels_count < channels_count)
2412 {
2413 _Channels.reserve(channels_count); // Avoid over reserving since this is likely to stay stable
2414 _Channels.resize(channels_count);
2415 }
2416 _Count = channels_count;
2417
2418 // Channels[] (24/32 bytes each) hold storage that we'll swap with draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2419 // The content of Channels[0] at this point doesn't matter. We clear it to make state tidy in a debugger but we
2420 // don't strictly need to. When we switch to the next channel, we'll copy draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer into
2421 // Channels[0] and then Channels[1] into draw_list->CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2422 memset(&_Channels[0], 0, sizeof(ImDrawChannel));
2423 for (int i = 1; i < channels_count; i++)
2424 {
2425 if (i >= old_channels_count)
2426 {
2427 IM_PLACEMENT_NEW(&_Channels[i]) ImDrawChannel();
2428 }
2429 else
2430 {
2431 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.resize(0);
2432 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2433 }
2434 }
2435}
2436
2437void ImDrawListSplitter::Merge(ImDrawList *draw_list)
2438{
2439 // Note that we never use or rely on _Channels.Size because it is merely a buffer that we never shrink back to 0 to
2440 // keep all sub-buffers ready for use.
2441 if (_Count <= 1)
2442 return;
2443
2444 SetCurrentChannel(draw_list, 0);
2445 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2446
2447 // Calculate our final buffer sizes. Also fix the incorrect IdxOffset values in each command.
2448 int new_cmd_buffer_count = 0;
2449 int new_idx_buffer_count = 0;
2450 ImDrawCmd *last_cmd = (_Count > 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size > 0) ? &draw_list->CmdBuffer.back() : NULL;
2451 int idx_offset = last_cmd ? last_cmd->IdxOffset + last_cmd->ElemCount : 0;
2452 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2453 {
2454 ImDrawChannel &ch = _Channels[i];
2455 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().ElemCount == 0 &&
2456 ch._CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL) // Equivalent of PopUnusedDrawCmd()
2457 ch._CmdBuffer.pop_back();
2458
2459 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && last_cmd != NULL)
2460 {
2461 // Do not include ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset() in the compare as we rebuild IdxOffset values
2462 // ourselves. Manipulating IdxOffset (e.g. by reordering draw commands like done by
2463 // RenderDimmedBackgroundBehindWindow()) is not supported within a splitter.
2464 ImDrawCmd *next_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer[0];
2465 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(last_cmd, next_cmd) == 0 && last_cmd->UserCallback == NULL &&
2466 next_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
2467 {
2468 // Merge previous channel last draw command with current channel first draw command if matching.
2469 last_cmd->ElemCount += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2470 idx_offset += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2471 ch._CmdBuffer.erase(ch._CmdBuffer.Data); // FIXME-OPT: Improve for multiple merges.
2472 }
2473 }
2474 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
2475 last_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer.back();
2476 new_cmd_buffer_count += ch._CmdBuffer.Size;
2477 new_idx_buffer_count += ch._IdxBuffer.Size;
2478 for (int cmd_n = 0; cmd_n < ch._CmdBuffer.Size; cmd_n++)
2479 {
2480 ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].IdxOffset = idx_offset;
2481 idx_offset += ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].ElemCount;
2482 }
2483 }
2484 draw_list->CmdBuffer.resize(draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size + new_cmd_buffer_count);
2485 draw_list->IdxBuffer.resize(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + new_idx_buffer_count);
2486
2487 // Write commands and indices in order (they are fairly small structures, we don't copy vertices only indices)
2488 ImDrawCmd *cmd_write = draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data + draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - new_cmd_buffer_count;
2489 ImDrawIdx *idx_write = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size - new_idx_buffer_count;
2490 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2491 {
2492 ImDrawChannel &ch = _Channels[i];
2493 if (int sz = ch._CmdBuffer.Size)
2494 {
2495 memcpy(cmd_write, ch._CmdBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawCmd));
2496 cmd_write += sz;
2497 }
2498 if (int sz = ch._IdxBuffer.Size)
2499 {
2500 memcpy(idx_write, ch._IdxBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawIdx));
2501 idx_write += sz;
2502 }
2503 }
2504 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
2505
2506 // Ensure there's always a non-callback draw command trailing the command-buffer
2507 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback != NULL)
2508 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2509
2510 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2511 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd = &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2512 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2513 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2514 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2515 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2516
2517 _Count = 1;
2518}
2519
2520void ImDrawListSplitter::SetCurrentChannel(ImDrawList *draw_list, int idx)
2521{
2522 IM_ASSERT(idx >= 0 && idx < _Count);
2523 if (_Current == idx)
2524 return;
2525
2526 // Overwrite ImVector (12/16 bytes), four times. This is merely a silly optimization instead of doing .swap()
2527 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._CmdBuffer, &draw_list->CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2528 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._IdxBuffer, &draw_list->IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2529 _Current = idx;
2530 memcpy(&draw_list->CmdBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2531 memcpy(&draw_list->IdxBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2532 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2533
2534 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2535 ImDrawCmd *curr_cmd =
2536 (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0) ? NULL : &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2537 if (curr_cmd == NULL)
2538 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2539 else if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2540 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2541 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2542 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2543}
2544
2545//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2546// [SECTION] ImDrawData
2547//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2548
2549void ImDrawData::Clear()
2550{
2551 Valid = false;
2552 CmdListsCount = TotalIdxCount = TotalVtxCount = 0;
2553 CmdLists.resize(0); // The ImDrawList are NOT owned by ImDrawData but e.g. by ImGuiContext, so we don't clear them.
2554 DisplayPos = DisplaySize = FramebufferScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2555 OwnerViewport = NULL;
2556}
2557
2558// Important: 'out_list' is generally going to be draw_data->CmdLists, but may be another temporary list
2559// as long at it is expected that the result will be later merged into draw_data->CmdLists[].
2560void ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(ImDrawData *draw_data, ImVector<ImDrawList *> *out_list, ImDrawList *draw_list)
2561{
2562 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0)
2563 return;
2564 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 1 && draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].ElemCount == 0 &&
2565 draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].UserCallback == NULL)
2566 return;
2567
2568 // Draw list sanity check. Detect mismatch between PrimReserve() calls and incrementing _VtxCurrentIdx, _VtxWritePtr
2569 // etc. May trigger for you if you are using PrimXXX functions incorrectly.
2570 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size == 0 ||
2571 draw_list->_VtxWritePtr == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2572 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size == 0 ||
2573 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr == draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2574 if (!(draw_list->Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
2575 IM_ASSERT((int)draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2576
2577 // Check that draw_list doesn't use more vertices than indexable (default ImDrawIdx = unsigned short = 2 bytes = 64K
2578 // vertices per ImDrawList = per window) If this assert triggers because you are drawing lots of stuff manually:
2579 // - First, make sure you are coarse clipping yourself and not trying to draw many things outside visible bounds.
2580 // Be mindful that the lower-level ImDrawList API doesn't filter vertices. Use the Metrics/Debugger window to
2581 // inspect draw list contents.
2582 // - If you want large meshes with more than 64K vertices, you can either:
2583 // (A) Handle the ImDrawCmd::VtxOffset value in your renderer backend, and set 'io.BackendFlags |=
2584 // ImGuiBackendFlags_RendererHasVtxOffset'.
2585 // Most example backends already support this from 1.71. Pre-1.71 backends won't.
2586 // Some graphics API such as GL ES 1/2 don't have a way to offset the starting vertex so it is not supported
2587 // for them.
2588 // (B) Or handle 32-bit indices in your renderer backend, and uncomment '#define ImDrawIdx unsigned int' line in
2589 // imconfig.h.
2590 // Most example backends already support this. For example, the OpenGL example code detect index size at
2591 // compile-time:
2592 // glDrawElements(GL_TRIANGLES, (GLsizei)pcmd->ElemCount, sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 ? GL_UNSIGNED_SHORT :
2593 // GL_UNSIGNED_INT, idx_buffer_offset);
2594 // Your own engine or render API may use different parameters or function calls to specify index sizes.
2595 // 2 and 4 bytes indices are generally supported by most graphics API.
2596 // - If for some reason neither of those solutions works for you, a workaround is to call BeginChild()/EndChild()
2597 // before reaching
2598 // the 64K limit to split your draw commands in multiple draw lists.
2599 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2)
2600 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx < (1 << 16) &&
2601 "Too many vertices in ImDrawList using 16-bit indices. Read comment above");
2602
2603 // Resolve callback data pointers
2604 if (draw_list->_CallbacksDataBuf.Size > 0)
2605 for (ImDrawCmd &cmd : draw_list->CmdBuffer)
2606 if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL && cmd.UserCallbackDataOffset != -1 && cmd.UserCallbackDataSize > 0)
2607 cmd.UserCallbackData = draw_list->_CallbacksDataBuf.Data + cmd.UserCallbackDataOffset;
2608
2609 // Add to output list + records state in ImDrawData
2610 out_list->push_back(draw_list);
2611 draw_data->CmdListsCount++;
2612 draw_data->TotalVtxCount += draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2613 draw_data->TotalIdxCount += draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2614}
2615
2616void ImDrawData::AddDrawList(ImDrawList *draw_list)
2617{
2618 IM_ASSERT(CmdLists.Size == CmdListsCount);
2619 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2620 ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(this, &CmdLists, draw_list);
2621}
2622
2623// For backward compatibility: convert all buffers from indexed to de-indexed, in case you cannot render indexed. Note:
2624// this is slow and most likely a waste of resources. Always prefer indexed rendering!
2625void ImDrawData::DeIndexAllBuffers()
2626{
2627 ImVector<ImDrawVert> new_vtx_buffer;
2628 TotalVtxCount = TotalIdxCount = 0;
2629 for (int i = 0; i < CmdListsCount; i++)
2630 {
2631 ImDrawList *cmd_list = CmdLists[i];
2632 if (cmd_list->IdxBuffer.empty())
2633 continue;
2634 new_vtx_buffer.resize(cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2635 for (int j = 0; j < cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size; j++)
2636 new_vtx_buffer[j] = cmd_list->VtxBuffer[cmd_list->IdxBuffer[j]];
2637 cmd_list->VtxBuffer.swap(new_vtx_buffer);
2638 cmd_list->IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2639 TotalVtxCount += cmd_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2640 }
2641}
2642
2643// Helper to scale the ClipRect field of each ImDrawCmd.
2644// Use if your final output buffer is at a different scale than draw_data->DisplaySize,
2645// or if there is a difference between your window resolution and framebuffer resolution.
2646void ImDrawData::ScaleClipRects(const ImVec2 &fb_scale)
2647{
2648 for (ImDrawList *draw_list : CmdLists)
2649 for (ImDrawCmd &cmd : draw_list->CmdBuffer)
2650 cmd.ClipRect = ImVec4(cmd.ClipRect.x * fb_scale.x, cmd.ClipRect.y * fb_scale.y, cmd.ClipRect.z * fb_scale.x,
2651 cmd.ClipRect.w * fb_scale.y);
2652}
2653
2654//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2655// [SECTION] Helpers ShadeVertsXXX functions
2656//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2657
2658// Generic linear color gradient, write to RGB fields, leave A untouched.
2659void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearColorGradientKeepAlpha(ImDrawList *draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx,
2660 ImVec2 gradient_p0, ImVec2 gradient_p1, ImU32 col0, ImU32 col1)
2661{
2662 ImVec2 gradient_extent = gradient_p1 - gradient_p0;
2663 float gradient_inv_length2 = 1.0f / ImLengthSqr(gradient_extent);
2664 ImDrawVert *vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2665 ImDrawVert *vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2666 const int col0_r = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2667 const int col0_g = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2668 const int col0_b = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2669 const int col_delta_r = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_r;
2670 const int col_delta_g = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_g;
2671 const int col_delta_b = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_b;
2672 for (ImDrawVert *vert = vert_start; vert < vert_end; vert++)
2673 {
2674 float d = ImDot(vert->pos - gradient_p0, gradient_extent);
2675 float t = ImClamp(d * gradient_inv_length2, 0.0f, 1.0f);
2676 int r = (int)(col0_r + col_delta_r * t);
2677 int g = (int)(col0_g + col_delta_g * t);
2678 int b = (int)(col0_b + col_delta_b * t);
2679 vert->col =
2680 (r << IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) | (g << IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) | (b << IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) | (vert->col & IM_COL32_A_MASK);
2681 }
2682}
2683
2684// Distribute UV over (a, b) rectangle
2685void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(ImDrawList *draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2 &a,
2686 const ImVec2 &b, const ImVec2 &uv_a, const ImVec2 &uv_b, bool clamp)
2687{
2688 const ImVec2 size = b - a;
2689 const ImVec2 uv_size = uv_b - uv_a;
2690 const ImVec2 scale =
2691 ImVec2(size.x != 0.0f ? (uv_size.x / size.x) : 0.0f, size.y != 0.0f ? (uv_size.y / size.y) : 0.0f);
2692
2693 ImDrawVert *vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2694 ImDrawVert *vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2695 if (clamp)
2696 {
2697 const ImVec2 min = ImMin(uv_a, uv_b);
2698 const ImVec2 max = ImMax(uv_a, uv_b);
2699 for (ImDrawVert *vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2700 vertex->uv = ImClamp(uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale), min, max);
2701 }
2702 else
2703 {
2704 for (ImDrawVert *vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2705 vertex->uv = uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale);
2706 }
2707}
2708
2709void ImGui::ShadeVertsTransformPos(ImDrawList *draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2 &pivot_in,
2710 float cos_a, float sin_a, const ImVec2 &pivot_out)
2711{
2712 ImDrawVert *vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2713 ImDrawVert *vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2714 for (ImDrawVert *vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2715 vertex->pos = ImRotate(vertex->pos - pivot_in, cos_a, sin_a) + pivot_out;
2716}

2722ImFontConfig::ImFontConfig()

2726 OversampleH = 0; // Auto == 1 or 2 depending on size
2727 OversampleV = 0; // Auto == 1
2728 GlyphMaxAdvanceX = FLT_MAX;
2729 RasterizerMultiply = 1.0f;
2730 RasterizerDensity = 1.0f;
2731 EllipsisChar = 0;
2732}

2829 " - XX XX - "
2830 " "};
2831

2849ImFontAtlas::ImFontAtlas()
2850{
2851 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
2852 TexGlyphPadding = 1;
2853 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
2854}
2855
2856ImFontAtlas::~ImFontAtlas()
2857{
2858 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2859 Clear();
2860}
2861
2862void ImFontAtlas::ClearInputData()
2863{
2864 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2865 for (ImFontConfig &font_cfg : Sources)
2866 if (font_cfg.FontData && font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2867 {
2868 IM_FREE(font_cfg.FontData);
2869 font_cfg.FontData = NULL;
2870 }
2871
2872 // When clearing this we lose access to the font name and other information used to build the font.
2873 for (ImFont *font : Fonts)
2874 if (font->Sources >= Sources.Data && font->Sources < Sources.Data + Sources.Size)
2875 {
2876 font->Sources = NULL;
2877 font->SourcesCount = 0;
2878 }
2879 Sources.clear();
2880 CustomRects.clear();
2881 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
2882 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2883}
2884
2885void ImFontAtlas::ClearTexData()
2886{
2887 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2888 if (TexPixelsAlpha8)
2889 IM_FREE(TexPixelsAlpha8);
2890 if (TexPixelsRGBA32)
2891 IM_FREE(TexPixelsRGBA32);
2892 TexPixelsAlpha8 = NULL;
2893 TexPixelsRGBA32 = NULL;
2894 TexPixelsUseColors = false;
2895 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2896}
2897
2898void ImFontAtlas::ClearFonts()
2899{
2900 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2901 ClearInputData();
2902 Fonts.clear_delete();
2903 TexReady = false;
2904}
2905
2906void ImFontAtlas::Clear()
2907{
2908 ClearInputData();
2909 ClearTexData();
2910 ClearFonts();
2911}
2912
2913void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsAlpha8(unsigned char **out_pixels, int *out_width, int *out_height,
2914 int *out_bytes_per_pixel)
2915{
2916 // Build atlas on demand
2917 if (TexPixelsAlpha8 == NULL)
2918 Build();
2919
2920 *out_pixels = TexPixelsAlpha8;
2921 if (out_width)
2922 *out_width = TexWidth;
2923 if (out_height)
2924 *out_height = TexHeight;
2925 if (out_bytes_per_pixel)
2926 *out_bytes_per_pixel = 1;
2927}
2928
2929void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsRGBA32(unsigned char **out_pixels, int *out_width, int *out_height,
2930 int *out_bytes_per_pixel)
2931{
2932 // Convert to RGBA32 format on demand
2933 // Although it is likely to be the most commonly used format, our font rendering is 1 channel / 8 bpp
2934 if (!TexPixelsRGBA32)
2935 {
2936 unsigned char *pixels = NULL;
2937 GetTexDataAsAlpha8(&pixels, NULL, NULL);
2938 if (pixels)
2939 {
2940 TexPixelsRGBA32 = (unsigned int *)IM_ALLOC((size_t)TexWidth * (size_t)TexHeight * 4);
2941 const unsigned char *src = pixels;
2942 unsigned int *dst = TexPixelsRGBA32;
2943 for (int n = TexWidth * TexHeight; n > 0; n--)
2944 *dst++ = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, (unsigned int)(*src++));
2945 }
2946 }
2947
2948 *out_pixels = (unsigned char *)TexPixelsRGBA32;
2949 if (out_width)
2950 *out_width = TexWidth;
2951 if (out_height)
2952 *out_height = TexHeight;
2953 if (out_bytes_per_pixel)
2954 *out_bytes_per_pixel = 4;
2955}
2956
2957ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFont(const ImFontConfig *font_cfg)
2958{
2959 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2960 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->FontData != NULL && font_cfg->FontDataSize > 0);
2961 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->SizePixels > 0.0f && "Is ImFontConfig struct correctly initialized?");
2962 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->RasterizerDensity > 0.0f && "Is ImFontConfig struct correctly initialized?");
2963
2964 // Create new font
2965 if (!font_cfg->MergeMode)
2966 Fonts.push_back(IM_NEW(ImFont));
2967 else
2968 IM_ASSERT(Fonts.Size > 0 &&
2969 "Cannot use MergeMode for the first font"); // When using MergeMode make sure that a font has already
2970 // been added before. You can use
2971 // ImGui::GetIO().Fonts->AddFontDefault() to add the
2972 // default imgui font.
2973
2974 Sources.push_back(*font_cfg);
2975 ImFontConfig &new_font_cfg = Sources.back();
2976 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont == NULL)
2977 new_font_cfg.DstFont = Fonts.back();
2978 if (!new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2979 {
2980 new_font_cfg.FontData = IM_ALLOC(new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2981 new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2982 memcpy(new_font_cfg.FontData, font_cfg->FontData, (size_t)new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2983 }
2984
2985 // Round font size
2986 // - We started rounding in 1.90 WIP (18991) as our layout system currently doesn't support non-rounded font size
2987 // well yet.
2988 // - Note that using io.FontGlobalScale or SetWindowFontScale(), with are legacy-ish, partially supported features,
2989 // can still lead to unrounded sizes.
2990 // - We may support it better later and remove this rounding.
2991 new_font_cfg.SizePixels = ImTrunc(new_font_cfg.SizePixels);
2992
2993 // Pointers to Sources data are otherwise dangling
2994 ImFontAtlasUpdateSourcesPointers(this);
2995
2996 // Invalidate texture
2997 TexReady = false;
2998 ClearTexData();
2999 return new_font_cfg.DstFont;
3000}
3001
3002// Default font TTF is compressed with stb_compress then base85 encoded (see misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp for
3003// encoder)
3004static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char *input);
3005static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char *output, const unsigned char *input, unsigned int length);
3006static unsigned int Decode85Byte(char c)
3007{
3008 return c >= '\\' ? c - 36 : c - 35;
3009}
3010static void Decode85(const unsigned char *src, unsigned char *dst)
3011{
3012 while (*src)
3013 {
3014 unsigned int tmp = Decode85Byte(src[0]) +
3015 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[1]) +
3016 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[2]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[3]) + 85 * Decode85Byte(src[4]))));
3017 dst[0] = ((tmp >> 0) & 0xFF);
3018 dst[1] = ((tmp >> 8) & 0xFF);
3019 dst[2] = ((tmp >> 16) & 0xFF);
3020 dst[3] = ((tmp >> 24) & 0xFF); // We can't assume little-endianness.
3021 src += 5;
3022 dst += 4;
3023 }
3024}
3025#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
3026static const char *GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTF(int *out_size);
3027#endif
3028
3029// Load embedded ProggyClean.ttf at size 13, disable oversampling
3030ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFontDefault(const ImFontConfig *font_cfg_template)
3031{
3032#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
3033 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
3034 if (!font_cfg_template)
3035 {
3036 font_cfg.OversampleH = font_cfg.OversampleV = 1;
3037 font_cfg.PixelSnapH = true;
3038 }
3039 if (font_cfg.SizePixels <= 0.0f)
3040 font_cfg.SizePixels = 13.0f * 1.0f;
3041 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
3042 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "ProggyClean.ttf, %dpx", (int)font_cfg.SizePixels);
3043 font_cfg.EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)0x0085;
3044 font_cfg.GlyphOffset.y = 1.0f * IM_TRUNC(font_cfg.SizePixels / 13.0f); // Add +1 offset per 13 units
3045
3046 int ttf_compressed_size = 0;
3047 const char *ttf_compressed = GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTF(&ttf_compressed_size);
3048 const ImWchar *glyph_ranges = font_cfg.GlyphRanges != NULL ? font_cfg.GlyphRanges : GetGlyphRangesDefault();
3049 ImFont *font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(ttf_compressed, ttf_compressed_size, font_cfg.SizePixels, &font_cfg,
3050 glyph_ranges);
3051 return font;
3052#else
3053 IM_ASSERT(0 && "AddFontDefault() disabled in this build.");
3054 IM_UNUSED(font_cfg_template);
3055 return NULL;
3056#endif // #ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_DEFAULT_FONT
3057}
3058
3059ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromFileTTF(const char *filename, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig *font_cfg_template,
3060 const ImWchar *glyph_ranges)
3061{
3062 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
3063 size_t data_size = 0;
3064 void *data = ImFileLoadToMemory(filename, "rb", &data_size, 0);
3065 if (!data)
3066 {
3067 IM_ASSERT_USER_ERROR(0, "Could not load font file!");
3068 return NULL;
3069 }
3070 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
3071 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
3072 {
3073 // Store a short copy of filename into into the font name for convenience
3074 const char *p;
3075 for (p = filename + ImStrlen(filename); p > filename && p[-1] != '/' && p[-1] != '\\'; p--)
3076 {
3077 }
3078 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "%s, %.0fpx", p, size_pixels);
3079 }
3080 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(data, (int)data_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
3081}
3082
3083// NB: Transfer ownership of 'ttf_data' to ImFontAtlas, unless font_cfg_template->FontDataOwnedByAtlas == false. Owned
3084// TTF buffer will be deleted after Build().
3085ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryTTF(void *font_data, int font_data_size, float size_pixels,
3086 const ImFontConfig *font_cfg_template, const ImWchar *glyph_ranges)
3087{
3088 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
3089 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
3090 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
3091 IM_ASSERT(font_data_size > 100 &&
3092 "Incorrect value for font_data_size!"); // Heuristic to prevent accidentally passing a wrong value to
3093 // font_data_size.
3094 font_cfg.FontData = font_data;
3095 font_cfg.FontDataSize = font_data_size;
3096 font_cfg.SizePixels = size_pixels > 0.0f ? size_pixels : font_cfg.SizePixels;
3097 if (glyph_ranges)
3098 font_cfg.GlyphRanges = glyph_ranges;
3099 return AddFont(&font_cfg);
3100}
3101
3102ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(const void *compressed_ttf_data, int compressed_ttf_size,
3103 float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig *font_cfg_template,
3104 const ImWchar *glyph_ranges)
3105{
3106 const unsigned int buf_decompressed_size = stb_decompress_length((const unsigned char *)compressed_ttf_data);
3107 unsigned char *buf_decompressed_data = (unsigned char *)IM_ALLOC(buf_decompressed_size);
3108 stb_decompress(buf_decompressed_data, (const unsigned char *)compressed_ttf_data,
3109 (unsigned int)compressed_ttf_size);
3110
3111 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
3112 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
3113 font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
3114 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(buf_decompressed_data, (int)buf_decompressed_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg,
3115 glyph_ranges);
3116}
3117
3118ImFont *ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(const char *compressed_ttf_data_base85, float size_pixels,
3119 const ImFontConfig *font_cfg, const ImWchar *glyph_ranges)
3120{
3121 int compressed_ttf_size = (((int)ImStrlen(compressed_ttf_data_base85) + 4) / 5) * 4;
3122 void *compressed_ttf = IM_ALLOC((size_t)compressed_ttf_size);
3123 Decode85((const unsigned char *)compressed_ttf_data_base85, (unsigned char *)compressed_ttf);
3124 ImFont *font =
3125 AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(compressed_ttf, compressed_ttf_size, size_pixels, font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
3126 IM_FREE(compressed_ttf);
3127 return font;
3128}

3141int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectFontGlyph(ImFont *font, ImWchar id, int width, int height, float advance_x,
3142 const ImVec2 &offset)
3143{
3144#ifdef IMGUI_USE_WCHAR32
3145 IM_ASSERT(id <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX);
3146#endif
3147 IM_ASSERT(font != NULL);
3148 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
3149 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
3150 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
3151 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
3152 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
3153 r.GlyphID = id;
3154 r.GlyphColored = 0; // Set to 1 manually to mark glyph as colored // FIXME: No official API for that (#8133)
3155 r.GlyphAdvanceX = advance_x;
3156 r.GlyphOffset = offset;
3157 r.Font = font;
3158 CustomRects.push_back(r);
3159 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
3160}

3162void ImFontAtlas::CalcCustomRectUV(const ImFontAtlasCustomRect *rect, ImVec2 *out_uv_min, ImVec2 *out_uv_max) const
3163{
3164 IM_ASSERT(TexWidth > 0 && TexHeight > 0); // Font atlas needs to be built before we can calculate UV coordinates
3165 IM_ASSERT(rect->IsPacked()); // Make sure the rectangle has been packed
3166 *out_uv_min = ImVec2((float)rect->X * TexUvScale.x, (float)rect->Y * TexUvScale.y);
3167 *out_uv_max = ImVec2((float)(rect->X + rect->Width) * TexUvScale.x, (float)(rect->Y + rect->Height) * TexUvScale.y);
3168}
3169
3170bool ImFontAtlasGetMouseCursorTexData(ImFontAtlas *atlas, ImGuiMouseCursor cursor_type, ImVec2 *out_offset,
3171 ImVec2 *out_size, ImVec2 out_uv_border[2], ImVec2 out_uv_fill[2])
3172{
3173 if (cursor_type <= ImGuiMouseCursor_None || cursor_type >= ImGuiMouseCursor_COUNT)
3174 return false;
3175 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
3176 return false;
3177
3178 IM_ASSERT(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors != -1);
3179 ImFontAtlasCustomRect *r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
3180 ImVec2 pos = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][0] + ImVec2((float)r->X, (float)r->Y);
3181 ImVec2 size = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][1];
3182 *out_size = size;
3183 *out_offset = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][2];
3184 out_uv_border[0] = (pos)*atlas->TexUvScale;
3185 out_uv_border[1] = (pos + size) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3186 pos.x += FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
3187 out_uv_fill[0] = (pos)*atlas->TexUvScale;
3188 out_uv_fill[1] = (pos + size) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3189 return true;
3190}
3191
3192bool ImFontAtlas::Build()
3193{
3194 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
3195
3196 // Default font is none are specified
3197 if (Sources.Size == 0)
3198 AddFontDefault();
3199
3200 // Select builder
3201 // - Note that we do not reassign to atlas->FontBuilderIO, since it is likely to point to static data which
3202 // may mess with some hot-reloading schemes. If you need to assign to this (for dynamic selection) AND are
3203 // using a hot-reloading scheme that messes up static data, store your own instance of ImFontBuilderIO somewhere
3204 // and point to it instead of pointing directly to return value of the GetBuilderXXX functions.
3205 const ImFontBuilderIO *builder_io = FontBuilderIO;
3206 if (builder_io == NULL)
3207 {
3208#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_FREETYPE
3209 builder_io = ImGuiFreeType::GetBuilderForFreeType();
3210#elif defined(IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE)
3211 builder_io = ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype();
3212#else
3213 IM_ASSERT(0); // Invalid Build function
3214#endif
3215 }
3216
3217 // Build
3218 return builder_io->FontBuilder_Build(this);
3219}
3220
3221void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(unsigned char out_table[256], float in_brighten_factor)
3222{
3223 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < 256; i++)
3224 {
3225 unsigned int value = (unsigned int)(i * in_brighten_factor);
3226 out_table[i] = value > 255 ? 255 : (value & 0xFF);
3227 }
3228}
3229
3230void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(const unsigned char table[256], unsigned char *pixels, int x, int y, int w,
3231 int h, int stride)
3232{
3233 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(w <= stride);
3234 unsigned char *data = pixels + x + y * stride;
3235 for (int j = h; j > 0; j--, data += stride - w)
3236 for (int i = w; i > 0; i--, data++)
3237 *data = table[*data];
3238}
3239
3240void ImFontAtlasBuildGetOversampleFactors(const ImFontConfig *src, int *out_oversample_h, int *out_oversample_v)
3241{
3242 // Automatically disable horizontal oversampling over size 36
3243 *out_oversample_h = (src->OversampleH != 0) ? src->OversampleH
3244 : (src->SizePixels * src->RasterizerDensity > 36.0f || src->PixelSnapH) ? 1
3245 : 2;
3246 *out_oversample_v = (src->OversampleV != 0) ? src->OversampleV : 1;
3247}
3248
3249#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
3250// Temporary data for one source font (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
3251// (C++03 doesn't allow instancing ImVector<> with function-local types so we declare the type here.)
3252struct ImFontBuildSrcData
3253{
3254 stbtt_fontinfo FontInfo;
3255 stbtt_pack_range PackRange; // Hold the list of codepoints to pack (essentially points to Codepoints.Data)
3256 stbrp_rect *Rects; // Rectangle to pack. We first fill in their size and the packer will give us their position.
3257 stbtt_packedchar *PackedChars; // Output glyphs
3258 const ImWchar *SrcRanges; // Ranges as requested by user (user is allowed to request too much, e.g. 0x0020..0xFFFF)
3259 int DstIndex; // Index into atlas->Fonts[] and dst_tmp_array[]
3260 int GlyphsHighest; // Highest requested codepoint
3261 int GlyphsCount; // Glyph count (excluding missing glyphs and glyphs already set by an earlier source font)
3262 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // Glyph bit map (random access, 1-bit per codepoint. This will be a maximum of 8KB)
3263 ImVector<int> GlyphsList; // Glyph codepoints list (flattened version of GlyphsSet)
3264};
3265
3266// Temporary data for one destination ImFont* (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
3267struct ImFontBuildDstData
3268{
3269 int SrcCount; // Number of source fonts targeting this destination font.
3270 int GlyphsHighest;
3271 int GlyphsCount;
3272 ImBitVector
3273 GlyphsSet; // This is used to resolve collision when multiple sources are merged into a same destination font.
3274};
3275
3276static void UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(const ImBitVector *in, ImVector<int> *out)
3277{
3278 IM_ASSERT(sizeof(in->Storage.Data[0]) == sizeof(int));
3279 const ImU32 *it_begin = in->Storage.begin();
3280 const ImU32 *it_end = in->Storage.end();
3281 for (const ImU32 *it = it_begin; it < it_end; it++)
3282 if (ImU32 entries_32 = *it)
3283 for (ImU32 bit_n = 0; bit_n < 32; bit_n++)
3284 if (entries_32 & ((ImU32)1 << bit_n))
3285 out->push_back((int)(((it - it_begin) << 5) + bit_n));
3286}
3287
3288static bool ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3289{
3290 IM_ASSERT(atlas->Sources.Size > 0);
3291
3292 ImFontAtlasBuildInit(atlas);
3293
3294 // Clear atlas
3295 atlas->TexID = (ImTextureID)NULL;
3296 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexHeight = 0;
3297 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
3298 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
3299 atlas->ClearTexData();
3300
3301 // Temporary storage for building
3302 ImVector<ImFontBuildSrcData> src_tmp_array;
3303 ImVector<ImFontBuildDstData> dst_tmp_array;
3304 src_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Sources.Size);
3305 dst_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Fonts.Size);
3306 memset(src_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)src_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
3307 memset(dst_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)dst_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
3308
3309 // 1. Initialize font loading structure, check font data validity
3310 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < atlas->Sources.Size; src_i++)
3311 {
3312 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3313 ImFontConfig &src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3314 IM_ASSERT(src.DstFont && (!src.DstFont->IsLoaded() || src.DstFont->ContainerAtlas == atlas));
3315
3316 // Find index from src.DstFont (we allow the user to set cfg.DstFont. Also it makes casual debugging nicer than
3317 // when storing indices)
3318 src_tmp.DstIndex = -1;
3319 for (int output_i = 0; output_i < atlas->Fonts.Size && src_tmp.DstIndex == -1; output_i++)
3320 if (src.DstFont == atlas->Fonts[output_i])
3321 src_tmp.DstIndex = output_i;
3322 if (src_tmp.DstIndex == -1)
3323 {
3324 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.DstIndex != -1); // src.DstFont not pointing within atlas->Fonts[] array?
3325 return false;
3326 }
3327 // Initialize helper structure for font loading and verify that the TTF/OTF data is correct
3328 const int font_offset = stbtt_GetFontOffsetForIndex((unsigned char *)src.FontData, src.FontNo);
3329 IM_ASSERT(font_offset >= 0 && "FontData is incorrect, or FontNo cannot be found.");
3330 if (!stbtt_InitFont(&src_tmp.FontInfo, (unsigned char *)src.FontData, font_offset))
3331 {
3332 IM_ASSERT(0 &&
3333 "stbtt_InitFont(): failed to parse FontData. It is correct and complete? Check FontDataSize.");
3334 return false;
3335 }
3336
3337 // Measure highest codepoints
3338 ImFontBuildDstData &dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
3339 src_tmp.SrcRanges = src.GlyphRanges ? src.GlyphRanges : atlas->GetGlyphRangesDefault();
3340 for (const ImWchar *src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
3341 {
3342 // Check for valid range. This may also help detect *some* dangling pointers, because a common
3343 // user error is to setup ImFontConfig::GlyphRanges with a pointer to data that isn't persistent,
3344 // or to forget to zero-terminate the glyph range array.
3345 IM_ASSERT(src_range[0] <= src_range[1] &&
3346 "Invalid range: is your glyph range array persistent? it is zero-terminated?");
3347 src_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest, (int)src_range[1]);
3348 }
3349 dst_tmp.SrcCount++;
3350 dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest, src_tmp.GlyphsHighest);
3351 }
3352
3353 // 2. For every requested codepoint, check for their presence in the font data, and handle redundancy or overlaps
3354 // between source fonts to avoid unused glyphs.
3355 int total_glyphs_count = 0;
3356 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3357 {
3358 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3359 ImFontBuildDstData &dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
3360 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
3361 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Storage.empty())
3362 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
3363
3364 for (const ImWchar *src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
3365 for (unsigned int codepoint = src_range[0]; codepoint <= src_range[1]; codepoint++)
3366 {
3367 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.TestBit(codepoint)) // Don't overwrite existing glyphs. We could make this an
3368 // option for MergeMode (e.g. MergeOverwrite==true)
3369 continue;
3370 if (!stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, codepoint)) // It is actually in the font?
3371 continue;
3372
3373 // Add to avail set/counters
3374 src_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
3375 dst_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
3376 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
3377 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
3378 total_glyphs_count++;
3379 }
3380 }
3381
3382 // 3. Unpack our bit map into a flat list (we now have all the Unicode points that we know are requested _and_
3383 // available _and_ not overlapping another)
3384 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3385 {
3386 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3387 src_tmp.GlyphsList.reserve(src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
3388 UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(&src_tmp.GlyphsSet, &src_tmp.GlyphsList);
3389 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Clear();
3390 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size == src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
3391 }
3392 for (int dst_i = 0; dst_i < dst_tmp_array.Size; dst_i++)
3393 dst_tmp_array[dst_i].GlyphsSet.Clear();
3394 dst_tmp_array.clear();
3395
3396 // Allocate packing character data and flag packed characters buffer as non-packed (x0=y0=x1=y1=0)
3397 // (We technically don't need to zero-clear buf_rects, but let's do it for the sake of sanity)
3398 ImVector<stbrp_rect> buf_rects;
3399 ImVector<stbtt_packedchar> buf_packedchars;
3400 buf_rects.resize(total_glyphs_count);
3401 buf_packedchars.resize(total_glyphs_count);
3402 memset(buf_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_rects.size_in_bytes());
3403 memset(buf_packedchars.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_packedchars.size_in_bytes());
3404
3405 // 4. Gather glyphs sizes so we can pack them in our virtual canvas.
3406 int total_surface = 0;
3407 int buf_rects_out_n = 0;
3408 int buf_packedchars_out_n = 0;
3409 const int pack_padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
3410 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3411 {
3412 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3413 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3414 continue;
3415
3416 src_tmp.Rects = &buf_rects[buf_rects_out_n];
3417 src_tmp.PackedChars = &buf_packedchars[buf_packedchars_out_n];
3418 buf_rects_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
3419 buf_packedchars_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
3420
3421 // Automatic selection of oversampling parameters
3422 ImFontConfig &src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3423 int oversample_h, oversample_v;
3424 ImFontAtlasBuildGetOversampleFactors(&src, &oversample_h, &oversample_v);
3425
3426 // Convert our ranges in the format stb_truetype wants
3427 src_tmp.PackRange.font_size = src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity;
3428 src_tmp.PackRange.first_unicode_codepoint_in_range = 0;
3429 src_tmp.PackRange.array_of_unicode_codepoints = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Data;
3430 src_tmp.PackRange.num_chars = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size;
3431 src_tmp.PackRange.chardata_for_range = src_tmp.PackedChars;
3432 src_tmp.PackRange.h_oversample = (unsigned char)oversample_h;
3433 src_tmp.PackRange.v_oversample = (unsigned char)oversample_v;
3434
3435 // Gather the sizes of all rectangles we will need to pack (this loop is based on
3436 // stbtt_PackFontRangesGatherRects)
3437 const float scale =
3438 (src.SizePixels > 0.0f)
3439 ? stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity)
3440 : stbtt_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels(&src_tmp.FontInfo, -src.SizePixels * src.RasterizerDensity);
3441 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size; glyph_i++)
3442 {
3443 int x0, y0, x1, y1;
3444 const int glyph_index_in_font = stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i]);
3445 IM_ASSERT(glyph_index_in_font != 0);
3446 stbtt_GetGlyphBitmapBoxSubpixel(&src_tmp.FontInfo, glyph_index_in_font, scale * oversample_h,
3447 scale * oversample_v, 0, 0, &x0, &y0, &x1, &y1);
3448 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w = (stbrp_coord)(x1 - x0 + pack_padding + oversample_h - 1);
3449 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h = (stbrp_coord)(y1 - y0 + pack_padding + oversample_v - 1);
3450 total_surface += src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w * src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h;
3451 }
3452 }
3453 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
3454 total_surface += (atlas->CustomRects[i].Width + pack_padding) * (atlas->CustomRects[i].Height + pack_padding);
3455
3456 // We need a width for the skyline algorithm, any width!
3457 // The exact width doesn't really matter much, but some API/GPU have texture size limitations and increasing width
3458 // can decrease height. User can override TexDesiredWidth and TexGlyphPadding if they wish, otherwise we use a
3459 // simple heuristic to select the width based on expected surface.
3460 const int surface_sqrt = (int)ImSqrt((float)total_surface) + 1;
3461 atlas->TexHeight = 0;
3462 if (atlas->TexDesiredWidth > 0)
3463 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexDesiredWidth;
3464 else
3465 atlas->TexWidth = (surface_sqrt >= 4096 * 0.7f) ? 4096
3466 : (surface_sqrt >= 2048 * 0.7f) ? 2048
3467 : (surface_sqrt >= 1024 * 0.7f) ? 1024
3468 : 512;
3469
3470 // 5. Start packing
3471 // Pack our extra data rectangles first, so it will be on the upper-left corner of our texture (UV will have small
3472 // values).
3473 const int TEX_HEIGHT_MAX = 1024 * 32;
3474 stbtt_pack_context spc = {};
3475 stbtt_PackBegin(&spc, NULL, atlas->TexWidth, TEX_HEIGHT_MAX, 0, 0, NULL);
3476 spc.padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding; // Because we mixup stbtt_PackXXX and stbrp_PackXXX there's a bit of a hack
3477 // here, not passing the value to stbtt_PackBegin() allows us to still pack a
3478 // TexWidth-1 wide item. (#8107)
3479 ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(atlas, spc.pack_info);
3480
3481 // 6. Pack each source font. No rendering yet, we are working with rectangles in an infinitely tall texture at this
3482 // point.
3483 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3484 {
3485 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3486 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3487 continue;
3488
3489 stbrp_pack_rects((stbrp_context *)spc.pack_info, src_tmp.Rects, src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
3490
3491 // Extend texture height and mark missing glyphs as non-packed so we won't render them.
3492 // FIXME: We are not handling packing failure here (would happen if we got off TEX_HEIGHT_MAX or if a single if
3493 // larger than TexWidth?)
3494 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
3495 if (src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].was_packed)
3496 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].y + src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h);
3497 }
3498
3499 // 7. Allocate texture
3500 atlas->TexHeight = (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoPowerOfTwoHeight) ? (atlas->TexHeight + 1)
3501 : ImUpperPowerOfTwo(atlas->TexHeight);
3502 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(1.0f / atlas->TexWidth, 1.0f / atlas->TexHeight);
3503 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 = (unsigned char *)IM_ALLOC(atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
3504 memset(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, 0, atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
3505 spc.pixels = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8;
3506 spc.height = atlas->TexHeight;
3507
3508 // 8. Render/rasterize font characters into the texture
3509 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3510 {
3511 ImFontConfig &src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3512 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3513 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
3514 continue;
3515
3516 stbtt_PackFontRangesRenderIntoRects(&spc, &src_tmp.FontInfo, &src_tmp.PackRange, 1, src_tmp.Rects);
3517
3518 // Apply multiply operator
3519 if (src.RasterizerMultiply != 1.0f)
3520 {
3521 unsigned char multiply_table[256];
3522 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(multiply_table, src.RasterizerMultiply);
3523 stbrp_rect *r = &src_tmp.Rects[0];
3524 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++, r++)
3525 if (r->was_packed)
3526 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(multiply_table, atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, r->x, r->y, r->w, r->h,
3527 atlas->TexWidth * 1);
3528 }
3529 src_tmp.Rects = NULL;
3530 }
3531
3532 // End packing
3533 stbtt_PackEnd(&spc);
3534 buf_rects.clear();
3535
3536 // 9. Setup ImFont and glyphs for runtime
3537 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
3538 {
3539 // When merging fonts with MergeMode=true:
3540 // - We can have multiple input fonts writing into a same destination font.
3541 // - dst_font->Sources is != from src which is our source configuration.
3542 ImFontBuildSrcData &src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
3543 ImFontConfig &src = atlas->Sources[src_i];
3544 ImFont *dst_font = src.DstFont;
3545
3546 const float font_scale = stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src.SizePixels);
3547 int unscaled_ascent, unscaled_descent, unscaled_line_gap;
3548 stbtt_GetFontVMetrics(&src_tmp.FontInfo, &unscaled_ascent, &unscaled_descent, &unscaled_line_gap);
3549
3550 const float ascent = ImCeil(unscaled_ascent * font_scale);
3551 const float descent = ImFloor(unscaled_descent * font_scale);
3552 ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(atlas, dst_font, &src, ascent, descent);
3553 const float font_off_x = src.GlyphOffset.x;
3554 const float font_off_y = src.GlyphOffset.y + IM_ROUND(dst_font->Ascent);
3555
3556 const float inv_rasterization_scale = 1.0f / src.RasterizerDensity;
3557
3558 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
3559 {
3560 // Register glyph
3561 const int codepoint = src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i];
3562 const stbtt_packedchar &pc = src_tmp.PackedChars[glyph_i];
3563 stbtt_aligned_quad q;
3564 float unused_x = 0.0f, unused_y = 0.0f;
3565 stbtt_GetPackedQuad(src_tmp.PackedChars, atlas->TexWidth, atlas->TexHeight, glyph_i, &unused_x, &unused_y,
3566 &q, 0);
3567 float x0 = q.x0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3568 float y0 = q.y0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3569 float x1 = q.x1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3570 float y1 = q.y1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3571 dst_font->AddGlyph(&src, (ImWchar)codepoint, x0, y0, x1, y1, q.s0, q.t0, q.s1, q.t1,
3572 pc.xadvance * inv_rasterization_scale);
3573 }
3574 }
3575
3576 // Cleanup
3577 src_tmp_array.clear_destruct();
3578
3579 ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(atlas);
3580 return true;
3581}
3582
3583const ImFontBuilderIO *ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype()
3584{
3585 static ImFontBuilderIO io;
3586 io.FontBuilder_Build = ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype;
3587 return &io;
3588}
3589
3590#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
3591
3592void ImFontAtlasUpdateSourcesPointers(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3593{
3594 for (ImFontConfig &src : atlas->Sources)
3595 {
3596 ImFont *font = src.DstFont;
3597 if (!src.MergeMode)
3598 {
3599 font->Sources = &src;
3600 font->SourcesCount = 0;
3601 }
3602 font->SourcesCount++;
3603 }
3604}
3605
3606void ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(ImFontAtlas *atlas, ImFont *font, ImFontConfig *font_config, float ascent, float descent)
3607{
3608 if (!font_config->MergeMode)
3609 {
3610 font->ClearOutputData();
3611 font->FontSize = font_config->SizePixels;
3612 IM_ASSERT(font->Sources == font_config);
3613 font->ContainerAtlas = atlas;
3614 font->Ascent = ascent;
3615 font->Descent = descent;
3616 }
3617}
3618
3619void ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(ImFontAtlas *atlas, void *stbrp_context_opaque)
3620{
3621 stbrp_context *pack_context = (stbrp_context *)stbrp_context_opaque;
3622 IM_ASSERT(pack_context != NULL);
3623
3624 ImVector<ImFontAtlasCustomRect> &user_rects = atlas->CustomRects;
3625 IM_ASSERT(user_rects.Size >=
3626 1); // We expect at least the default custom rects to be registered, else something went wrong.
3627#ifdef __GNUC__
3628 if (user_rects.Size < 1)
3629 {
3630 __builtin_unreachable();
3631 } // Workaround for GCC bug if IM_ASSERT() is defined to conditionally throw (see #5343)
3632#endif
3633
3634 const int pack_padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
3635 ImVector<stbrp_rect> pack_rects;
3636 pack_rects.resize(user_rects.Size);
3637 memset(pack_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)pack_rects.size_in_bytes());
3638 for (int i = 0; i < user_rects.Size; i++)
3639 {
3640 pack_rects[i].w = user_rects[i].Width + pack_padding;
3641 pack_rects[i].h = user_rects[i].Height + pack_padding;
3642 }
3643 stbrp_pack_rects(pack_context, &pack_rects[0], pack_rects.Size);
3644 for (int i = 0; i < pack_rects.Size; i++)
3645 if (pack_rects[i].was_packed)
3646 {
3647 user_rects[i].X = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].x;
3648 user_rects[i].Y = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].y;
3649 IM_ASSERT(pack_rects[i].w == user_rects[i].Width + pack_padding &&
3650 pack_rects[i].h == user_rects[i].Height + pack_padding);
3651 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, pack_rects[i].y + pack_rects[i].h);
3652 }
3653}
3654
3655void ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas *atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char *in_str,
3656 char in_marker_char, unsigned char in_marker_pixel_value)
3657{
3658 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3659 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3660 unsigned char *out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3661 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3662 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3663 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : 0x00;
3664}
3665
3666void ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas *atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char *in_str,
3667 char in_marker_char, unsigned int in_marker_pixel_value)
3668{
3669 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3670 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3671 unsigned int *out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3672 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3673 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3674 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : IM_COL32_BLACK_TRANS;
3675}
3676
3677static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3678{
3679 ImFontAtlasCustomRect *r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
3680 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3681
3682 const int w = atlas->TexWidth;
3683 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
3684 {
3685 // White pixels only
3686 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == 2 && r->Height == 2);
3687 const int offset = (int)r->X + (int)r->Y * w;
3688 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3689 {
3690 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w] =
3691 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w + 1] = 0xFF;
3692 }
3693 else
3694 {
3695 atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w] =
3696 atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w + 1] = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3697 }
3698 }
3699 else
3700 {
3701 // White pixels and mouse cursor
3702 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1 && r->Height == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3703 const int x_for_white = r->X;
3704 const int x_for_black = r->X + FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
3705 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3706 {
3707 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W,
3708 FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS,
3709 '.', 0xFF);
3710 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W,
3711 FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS,
3712 'X', 0xFF);
3713 }
3714 else
3715 {
3716 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W,
3717 FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS,
3718 '.', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3719 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W,
3720 FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS,
3721 'X', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3722 }
3723 }
3724 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2((r->X + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.x, (r->Y + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.y);
3725}
3726
3727static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3728{
3729 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines)
3730 return;
3731
3732 // This generates a triangular shape in the texture, with the various line widths stacked on top of each other to
3733 // allow interpolation between them
3734 ImFontAtlasCustomRect *r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdLines);
3735 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3736 for (int n = 0; n < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1; n++) // +1 because of the zero-width row
3737 {
3738 // Each line consists of at least two empty pixels at the ends, with a line of solid pixels in the middle
3739 int y = n;
3740 int line_width = n;
3741 int pad_left = (r->Width - line_width) / 2;
3742 int pad_right = r->Width - (pad_left + line_width);
3743
3744 // Write each slice
3745 IM_ASSERT(pad_left + line_width + pad_right == r->Width &&
3746 y < r->Height); // Make sure we're inside the texture bounds before we start writing pixels
3747 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3748 {
3749 unsigned char *write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3750 for (int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3751 *(write_ptr + i) = 0x00;
3752
3753 for (int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3754 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = 0xFF;
3755
3756 for (int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3757 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = 0x00;
3758 }
3759 else
3760 {
3761 unsigned int *write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3762 for (int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3763 *(write_ptr + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3764
3765 for (int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3766 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3767
3768 for (int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3769 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3770 }
3771
3772 // Calculate UVs for this line
3773 ImVec2 uv0 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left - 1), (float)(r->Y + y)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3774 ImVec2 uv1 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left + line_width + 1), (float)(r->Y + y + 1)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3775 float half_v =
3776 (uv0.y + uv1.y) * 0.5f; // Calculate a constant V in the middle of the row to avoid sampling artifacts
3777 atlas->TexUvLines[n] = ImVec4(uv0.x, half_v, uv1.x, half_v);
3778 }
3779}
3780
3781// Note: this is called / shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder
3782void ImFontAtlasBuildInit(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3783{
3784 // Register texture region for mouse cursors or standard white pixels
3785 if (atlas->PackIdMouseCursors < 0)
3786 {
3787 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
3788 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors =
3789 atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3790 else
3791 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(2, 2);
3792 }
3793
3794 // Register texture region for thick lines
3795 // The +2 here is to give space for the end caps, whilst height +1 is to accommodate the fact we have a zero-width
3796 // row
3797 if (atlas->PackIdLines < 0)
3798 {
3799 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines))
3800 atlas->PackIdLines =
3801 atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 2, IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1);
3802 }
3803}
3804
3805// This is called/shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder.
3806void ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(ImFontAtlas *atlas)
3807{
3808 // Render into our custom data blocks
3809 IM_ASSERT(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL || atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 != NULL);
3810 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(atlas);
3811 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(atlas);
3812
3813 // Register custom rectangle glyphs
3814 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
3815 {
3816 const ImFontAtlasCustomRect *r = &atlas->CustomRects[i];
3817 if (r->Font == NULL || r->GlyphID == 0)
3818 continue;
3819
3820 // Will ignore ImFontConfig settings: GlyphMinAdvanceX, GlyphMinAdvanceY, PixelSnapH
3821 IM_ASSERT(r->Font->ContainerAtlas == atlas);
3822 ImVec2 uv0, uv1;
3823 atlas->CalcCustomRectUV(r, &uv0, &uv1);
3824 r->Font->AddGlyph(NULL, (ImWchar)r->GlyphID, r->GlyphOffset.x, r->GlyphOffset.y, r->GlyphOffset.x + r->Width,
3825 r->GlyphOffset.y + r->Height, uv0.x, uv0.y, uv1.x, uv1.y, r->GlyphAdvanceX);
3826 if (r->GlyphColored)
3827 r->Font->Glyphs.back().Colored = 1;
3828 }
3829
3830 // Build all fonts lookup tables
3831 for (ImFont *font : atlas->Fonts)
3832 if (font->DirtyLookupTables)
3833 font->BuildLookupTable();
3834
3835 atlas->TexReady = true;
3836}

3838//-------------------------------------------------------------------------

3840//-------------------------------------------------------------------------

3842// - GetGlyphRangesGreek()

3844// - GetGlyphRangesChineseFull()
3845// - GetGlyphRangesChineseSimplifiedCommon()
3846// - GetGlyphRangesJapanese()
3847// - GetGlyphRangesCyrillic()
3848// - GetGlyphRangesThai()
3849// - GetGlyphRangesVietnamese()
3850//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3851
3852// Retrieve list of range (2 int per range, values are inclusive)
3853const ImWchar *ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesDefault()
3854{
3855 static const ImWchar ranges[] = {
3856 0x0020,
3857 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3858 0,
3859 };
3860 return &ranges[0];
3861}

3863const ImWchar *ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesGreek()
3864{
3865 static const ImWchar ranges[] = {
3866 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3867 0x0370, 0x03FF, // Greek and Coptic
3868 0,
3869 };
3870 return &ranges[0];
3871}
3872
3873const ImWchar *ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesKorean()
3874{
3875 static const ImWchar ranges[] = {
3876 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3877 0x3131, 0x3163, // Korean alphabets
3878 0xAC00, 0xD7A3, // Korean characters
3879 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD, // Invalid
3880 0,
3881 };
3882 return &ranges[0];
3883}
3884
3885const ImWchar *ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesChineseFull()
3886{
3887 static const ImWchar ranges[] = {
3888 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3889 0x2000, 0x206F, // General Punctuation
3890 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
3891 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
3892 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
3893 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD, // Invalid
3894 0x4e00, 0x9FAF, // CJK Ideograms
3895 0,
3896 };
3897 return &ranges[0];
3898}
3899
3900static void UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(int base_codepoint, const short *accumulative_offsets,
3901 int accumulative_offsets_count, ImWchar *out_ranges)
3902{
3903 for (int n = 0; n < accumulative_offsets_count; n++, out_ranges += 2)
3904 {
3905 out_ranges[0] = out_ranges[1] = (ImWchar)(base_codepoint + accumulative_offsets[n]);
3906 base_codepoint += accumulative_offsets[n];
3907 }
3908 out_ranges[0] = 0;
3909}

4025 47, 5, 21, 6};
4026 static ImWchar base_ranges[] = // not zero-terminated
4027 {
4028 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
4029 0x2000, 0x206F, // General Punctuation
4030 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
4031 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
4032 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
4033 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD // Invalid
4034 };
4035 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00) * 2 + 1] = {
4036 0};

4038 {
4039 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));
4040 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00,
4041 IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00),
4042 full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
4043 }

4045}
4046
4047const ImWchar *ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesJapanese()
4048{
4049 // 2999 ideograms code points for Japanese

4189 {

4191 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana

4196 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00) * 2 + 1] = {
4197 0};
4198 if (!full_ranges[0])
4199 {

4201 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00,
4202 IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00),
4203 full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
4204 }

4206}
