4241//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4242// [SECTION] ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder
4243//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4244
4245void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddText(const char *text, const char *text_end)
4246{
4247 while (text_end ? (text < text_end) : *text)
4248 {
4249 unsigned int c = 0;
4250 int c_len = ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, text, text_end);
4251 text += c_len;
4252 if (c_len == 0)
4253 break;
4254 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
4255 }
4256}
4257
4258void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddRanges(const ImWchar *ranges)
4259{
4260 for (; ranges[0]; ranges += 2)
4261 for (unsigned int c = ranges[0]; c <= ranges[1] && c <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX; c++) //-V560
4262 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
4263}
4264
4265void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::BuildRanges(ImVector<ImWchar> *out_ranges)
4266{
4267 const int max_codepoint = IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX;
4268 for (int n = 0; n <= max_codepoint; n++)
4269 if (GetBit(n))
4270 {
4271 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
4272 while (n < max_codepoint && GetBit(n + 1))
4273 n++;
4274 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
4275 }
4276 out_ranges->push_back(0);
4277}
4278
4279//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4280// [SECTION] ImFont
4281//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4282
4283ImFont::ImFont()
4284{
4285 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
4286 Scale = 1.0f;
4287}
4288
4289ImFont::~ImFont()
4290{
4291 ClearOutputData();
4292}
4293
4294void ImFont::ClearOutputData()
4295{
4296 FontSize = 0.0f;
4297 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
4298 Glyphs.clear();
4299 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
4300 IndexLookup.clear();
4301 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
4302 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
4303 DirtyLookupTables = true;
4304 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
4305 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
4306 memset(Used8kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used8kPagesMap));
4307}
4308
4309static ImWchar FindFirstExistingGlyph(ImFont *font, const ImWchar *candidate_chars, int candidate_chars_count)
4310{
4311 for (int n = 0; n < candidate_chars_count; n++)
4312 if (font->FindGlyphNoFallback(candidate_chars[n]) != NULL)
4313 return candidate_chars[n];
4314 return 0;
4315}
4316
4317void ImFont::BuildLookupTable()
4318{
4319 int max_codepoint = 0;
4320 for (int i = 0; i != Glyphs.Size; i++)
4321 max_codepoint = ImMax(max_codepoint, (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint);
4322
4323 // Build lookup table
4324 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size > 0 && "Font has not loaded glyph!");
4325 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // -1 is reserved
4326 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
4327 IndexLookup.clear();
4328 DirtyLookupTables = false;
4329 memset(Used8kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used8kPagesMap));
4330 GrowIndex(max_codepoint + 1);
4331 for (int i = 0; i < Glyphs.Size; i++)
4332 {
4333 int codepoint = (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint;
4334 IndexAdvanceX[codepoint] = Glyphs[i].AdvanceX;
4335 IndexLookup[codepoint] = (ImU16)i;
4336
4337 // Mark 4K page as used
4338 const int page_n = codepoint / 8192;
4339 Used8kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] |= 1 << (page_n & 7);
4340 }
4341
4342 // Create a glyph to handle TAB
4343 // FIXME: Needs proper TAB handling but it needs to be contextualized (or we could arbitrary say that each string
4344 // starts at "column 0" ?)
4345 if (FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
4346 {
4347 if (Glyphs.back().Codepoint != '\t') // So we can call this function multiple times (FIXME: Flaky)
4348 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
4349 ImFontGlyph &tab_glyph = Glyphs.back();
4350 tab_glyph = *FindGlyph((ImWchar)' ');
4351 tab_glyph.Codepoint = '\t';
4352 tab_glyph.AdvanceX *= IM_TABSIZE;
4353 IndexAdvanceX[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (float)tab_glyph.AdvanceX;
4354 IndexLookup[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (ImU16)(Glyphs.Size - 1);
4355 }
4356
4357 // Mark special glyphs as not visible (note that AddGlyph already mark as non-visible glyphs with zero-size
4358 // polygons)
4359 if (ImFontGlyph *glyph = (ImFontGlyph *)(void *)FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
4360 glyph->Visible = false;
4361 if (ImFontGlyph *glyph = (ImFontGlyph *)(void *)FindGlyph((ImWchar)'\t'))
4362 glyph->Visible = false;
4363
4364 // Setup Fallback character
4365 const ImWchar fallback_chars[] = {(ImWchar)IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_INVALID, (ImWchar)'?', (ImWchar)' '};
4366 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
4367 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
4368 {
4369 FallbackChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, fallback_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(fallback_chars));
4370 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
4371 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
4372 {
4373 FallbackGlyph = &Glyphs.back();
4374 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)FallbackGlyph->Codepoint;
4375 }
4376 }
4377 FallbackAdvanceX = FallbackGlyph->AdvanceX;
4378 for (int i = 0; i < max_codepoint + 1; i++)
4379 if (IndexAdvanceX[i] < 0.0f)
4380 IndexAdvanceX[i] = FallbackAdvanceX;
4381
4382 // Setup Ellipsis character. It is required for rendering elided text. We prefer using U+2026 (horizontal ellipsis).
4383 // However some old fonts may contain ellipsis at U+0085. Here we auto-detect most suitable ellipsis character.
4384 // FIXME: Note that 0x2026 is rarely included in our font ranges. Because of this we are more likely to use three
4385 // individual dots.
4386 const ImWchar ellipsis_chars[] = {Sources->EllipsisChar, (ImWchar)0x2026, (ImWchar)0x0085};
4387 const ImWchar dots_chars[] = {(ImWchar)'.', (ImWchar)0xFF0E};
4388 if (EllipsisChar == 0)
4389 EllipsisChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, ellipsis_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(ellipsis_chars));
4390 const ImWchar dot_char = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, dots_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(dots_chars));
4391 if (EllipsisChar != 0)
4392 {
4393 EllipsisCharCount = 1;
4394 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = FindGlyph(EllipsisChar)->X1;
4395 }
4396 else if (dot_char != 0)
4397 {
4398 const ImFontGlyph *dot_glyph = FindGlyph(dot_char);
4399 EllipsisChar = dot_char;
4400 EllipsisCharCount = 3;
4401 EllipsisCharStep = (float)(int)(dot_glyph->X1 - dot_glyph->X0) + 1.0f;
4402 EllipsisWidth = ImMax(dot_glyph->AdvanceX, dot_glyph->X0 + EllipsisCharStep * 3.0f -
4403 1.0f); // FIXME: Slightly odd for normally mono-space fonts but
4404 // since this is used for trailing contents.
4405 }
4406}
4407
4408// API is designed this way to avoid exposing the 8K page size
4409// e.g. use with IsGlyphRangeUnused(0, 255)
4410bool ImFont::IsGlyphRangeUnused(unsigned int c_begin, unsigned int c_last)
4411{
4412 unsigned int page_begin = (c_begin / 8192);
4413 unsigned int page_last = (c_last / 8192);
4414 for (unsigned int page_n = page_begin; page_n <= page_last; page_n++)
4415 if ((page_n >> 3) < sizeof(Used8kPagesMap))
4416 if (Used8kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] & (1 << (page_n & 7)))
4417 return false;
4418 return true;
4419}
4420
4421void ImFont::GrowIndex(int new_size)
4422{
4423 IM_ASSERT(IndexAdvanceX.Size == IndexLookup.Size);
4424 if (new_size <= IndexLookup.Size)
4425 return;
4426 IndexAdvanceX.resize(new_size, -1.0f);
4427 IndexLookup.resize(new_size, (ImU16)-1);
4428}
4429
4430// x0/y0/x1/y1 are offset from the character upper-left layout position, in pixels. Therefore x0/y0 are often fairly
4431// close to zero. Not to be mistaken with texture coordinates, which are held by u0/v0/u1/v1 in normalized format
4432// (0.0..1.0 on each texture axis). 'src' is not necessarily == 'this->Sources' because multiple source fonts+configs
4433// can be used to build one target font.
4434void ImFont::AddGlyph(const ImFontConfig *src, ImWchar codepoint, float x0, float y0, float x1, float y1, float u0,
4435 float v0, float u1, float v1, float advance_x)
4436{
4437 if (src != NULL)
4438 {
4439 // Clamp & recenter if needed
4440 const float advance_x_original = advance_x;
4441 advance_x = ImClamp(advance_x, src->GlyphMinAdvanceX, src->GlyphMaxAdvanceX);
4442 if (advance_x != advance_x_original)
4443 {
4444 float char_off_x = src->PixelSnapH ? ImTrunc((advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f)
4445 : (advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f;
4446 x0 += char_off_x;
4447 x1 += char_off_x;
4448 }
4449
4450 // Snap to pixel
4451 if (src->PixelSnapH)
4452 advance_x = IM_ROUND(advance_x);
4453
4454 // Bake extra spacing
4455 advance_x += src->GlyphExtraAdvanceX;
4456 }
4457
4458 int glyph_idx = Glyphs.Size;
4459 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
4460 ImFontGlyph &glyph = Glyphs[glyph_idx];
4461 glyph.Codepoint = (unsigned int)codepoint;
4462 glyph.Visible = (x0 != x1) && (y0 != y1);
4463 glyph.Colored = false;
4464 glyph.X0 = x0;
4465 glyph.Y0 = y0;
4466 glyph.X1 = x1;
4467 glyph.Y1 = y1;
4468 glyph.U0 = u0;
4469 glyph.V0 = v0;
4470 glyph.U1 = u1;
4471 glyph.V1 = v1;
4472 glyph.AdvanceX = advance_x;
4473 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // IndexLookup[] hold 16-bit values and -1 is reserved.
4474
4475 // Compute rough surface usage metrics (+1 to account for average padding, +0.99 to round)
4476 // We use (U1-U0)*TexWidth instead of X1-X0 to account for oversampling.
4477 float pad = ContainerAtlas->TexGlyphPadding + 0.99f;
4478 DirtyLookupTables = true;
4479 MetricsTotalSurface += (int)((glyph.U1 - glyph.U0) * ContainerAtlas->TexWidth + pad) *
4480 (int)((glyph.V1 - glyph.V0) * ContainerAtlas->TexHeight + pad);
4481}
4482
4483void ImFont::AddRemapChar(ImWchar dst, ImWchar src, bool overwrite_dst)
4484{
4485 IM_ASSERT(IndexLookup.Size > 0); // Currently this can only be called AFTER the font has been built, aka after
4486 // calling ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAs*() function.
4487 unsigned int index_size = (unsigned int)IndexLookup.Size;
4488
4489 if (dst < index_size && IndexLookup.Data[dst] == (ImU16)-1 && !overwrite_dst) // 'dst' already exists
4490 return;
4491 if (src >= index_size && dst >= index_size) // both 'dst' and 'src' don't exist -> no-op
4492 return;
4493
4494 GrowIndex(dst + 1);
4495 IndexLookup[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexLookup.Data[src] : (ImU16)-1;
4496 IndexAdvanceX[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[src] : 1.0f;
4497}
4498
4499// Find glyph, return fallback if missing
4500ImFontGlyph *ImFont::FindGlyph(ImWchar c)
4501{
4502 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
4503 return FallbackGlyph;
4504 const ImU16 i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
4505 if (i == (ImU16)-1)
4506 return FallbackGlyph;
4507 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
4508}
4509
4510ImFontGlyph *ImFont::FindGlyphNoFallback(ImWchar c)
4511{
4512 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
4513 return NULL;
4514 const ImU16 i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
4515 if (i == (ImU16)-1)
4516 return NULL;
4517 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
4518}
4519
4520// Trim trailing space and find beginning of next line
4521static inline const char *CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(const char *text, const char *text_end)
4522{
4523 while (text < text_end && ImCharIsBlankA(*text))
4524 text++;
4525 if (*text == '\n')
4526 text++;
4527 return text;
4528}
4529
4530#define ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(_FONT, _CH) \
4531 ((int)(_CH) < (_FONT)->IndexAdvanceX.Size ? (_FONT)->IndexAdvanceX.Data[_CH] : (_FONT)->FallbackAdvanceX)
4532
4533// Simple word-wrapping for English, not full-featured. Please submit failing cases!
4534// This will return the next location to wrap from. If no wrapping if necessary, this will fast-forward to e.g.
4535// text_end.
4536// FIXME: Much possible improvements (don't cut things like "word !", "word!!!" but cut within "word,,,,", more sensible
4537// support for punctuations, support for Unicode punctuations, etc.)
4538const char *ImFont::CalcWordWrapPositionA(float scale, const char *text, const char *text_end, float wrap_width)
4539{
4540 // For references, possible wrap point marked with ^
4541 // "aaa bbb, ccc,ddd. eee fff. ggg!"
4542 // ^ ^ ^ ^ ^__ ^ ^
4543
4544 // List of hardcoded separators: .,;!?'"
4545
4546 // Skip extra blanks after a line returns (that includes not counting them in width computation)
4547 // e.g. "Hello world" --> "Hello" "World"
4548
4549 // Cut words that cannot possibly fit within one line.
4550 // e.g.: "The tropical fish" with ~5 characters worth of width --> "The tr" "opical" "fish"
4551 float line_width = 0.0f;
4552 float word_width = 0.0f;
4553 float blank_width = 0.0f;
4554 wrap_width /= scale; // We work with unscaled widths to avoid scaling every characters
4555
4556 const char *word_end = text;
4557 const char *prev_word_end = NULL;
4558 bool inside_word = true;
4559
4560 const char *s = text;
4561 IM_ASSERT(text_end != NULL);
4562 while (s < text_end)
4563 {
4564 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4565 const char *next_s;
4566 if (c < 0x80)
4567 next_s = s + 1;
4568 else
4569 next_s = s + ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4570
4571 if (c < 32)
4572 {
4573 if (c == '\n')
4574 {
4575 line_width = word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
4576 inside_word = true;
4577 s = next_s;
4578 continue;
4579 }
4580 if (c == '\r')
4581 {
4582 s = next_s;
4583 continue;
4584 }
4585 }
4586
4587 const float char_width = ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(this, c);
4588 if (ImCharIsBlankW(c))
4589 {
4590 if (inside_word)
4591 {
4592 line_width += blank_width;
4593 blank_width = 0.0f;
4594 word_end = s;
4595 }
4596 blank_width += char_width;
4597 inside_word = false;
4598 }
4599 else
4600 {
4601 word_width += char_width;
4602 if (inside_word)
4603 {
4604 word_end = next_s;
4605 }
4606 else
4607 {
4608 prev_word_end = word_end;
4609 line_width += word_width + blank_width;
4610 word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
4611 }
4612
4613 // Allow wrapping after punctuation.
4614 inside_word = (c != '.' && c != ',' && c != ';' && c != '!' && c != '?' && c != '\"');
4615 }
4616
4617 // We ignore blank width at the end of the line (they can be skipped)
4618 if (line_width + word_width > wrap_width)
4619 {
4620 // Words that cannot possibly fit within an entire line will be cut anywhere.
4621 if (word_width < wrap_width)
4622 s = prev_word_end ? prev_word_end : word_end;
4623 break;
4624 }
4625
4626 s = next_s;
4627 }
4628
4629 // Wrap_width is too small to fit anything. Force displaying 1 character to minimize the height discontinuity.
4630 // +1 may not be a character start point in UTF-8 but it's ok because caller loops use (text >= word_wrap_eol).
4631 if (s == text && text < text_end)
4632 return s + 1;
4633 return s;
4634}
4635
4636ImVec2 ImFont::CalcTextSizeA(float size, float max_width, float wrap_width, const char *text_begin,
4637 const char *text_end, const char **remaining)
4638{
4639 if (!text_end)
4640 text_end = text_begin + ImStrlen(text_begin); // FIXME-OPT: Need to avoid this.
4641
4642 const float line_height = size;
4643 const float scale = size / FontSize;
4644
4645 ImVec2 text_size = ImVec2(0, 0);
4646 float line_width = 0.0f;
4647
4648 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
4649 const char *word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4650
4651 const char *s = text_begin;
4652 while (s < text_end)
4653 {
4654 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4655 {
4656 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not
4657 // intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
4658 if (!word_wrap_eol)
4659 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - line_width);
4660
4661 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
4662 {
4663 if (text_size.x < line_width)
4664 text_size.x = line_width;
4665 text_size.y += line_height;
4666 line_width = 0.0f;
4667 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4668 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
4669 continue;
4670 }
4671 }
4672
4673 // Decode and advance source
4674 const char *prev_s = s;
4675 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4676 if (c < 0x80)
4677 s += 1;
4678 else
4679 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4680
4681 if (c < 32)
4682 {
4683 if (c == '\n')
4684 {
4685 text_size.x = ImMax(text_size.x, line_width);
4686 text_size.y += line_height;
4687 line_width = 0.0f;
4688 continue;
4689 }
4690 if (c == '\r')
4691 continue;
4692 }
4693
4694 const float char_width = ImFontGetCharAdvanceX(this, c) * scale;
4695 if (line_width + char_width >= max_width)
4696 {
4697 s = prev_s;
4698 break;
4699 }
4700
4701 line_width += char_width;
4702 }
4703
4704 if (text_size.x < line_width)
4705 text_size.x = line_width;
4706
4707 if (line_width > 0 || text_size.y == 0.0f)
4708 text_size.y += line_height;
4709
4710 if (remaining)
4711 *remaining = s;
4712
4713 return text_size;
4714}
4715
4716// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
4717void ImFont::RenderChar(ImDrawList *draw_list, float size, const ImVec2 &pos, ImU32 col, ImWchar c)
4718{
4719 const ImFontGlyph *glyph = FindGlyph(c);
4720 if (!glyph || !glyph->Visible)
4721 return;
4722 if (glyph->Colored)
4723 col |= ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
4724 float scale = (size >= 0.0f) ? (size / FontSize) : 1.0f;
4725 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
4726 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
4727 draw_list->PrimReserve(6, 4);
4728 draw_list->PrimRectUV(ImVec2(x + glyph->X0 * scale, y + glyph->Y0 * scale),
4729 ImVec2(x + glyph->X1 * scale, y + glyph->Y1 * scale), ImVec2(glyph->U0, glyph->V0),
4730 ImVec2(glyph->U1, glyph->V1), col);
4731}
4732
4733// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
4734void ImFont::RenderText(ImDrawList *draw_list, float size, const ImVec2 &pos, ImU32 col, const ImVec4 &clip_rect,
4735 const char *text_begin, const char *text_end, float wrap_width, bool cpu_fine_clip)
4736{
4737 // Align to be pixel perfect
4738 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
4739 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
4740 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4741 return;
4742
4743 if (!text_end)
4744 text_end = text_begin + ImStrlen(text_begin); // ImGui:: functions generally already provides a valid text_end,
4745 // so this is merely to handle direct calls.
4746
4747 const float scale = size / FontSize;
4748 const float line_height = FontSize * scale;
4749 const float origin_x = x;
4750 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
4751
4752 // Fast-forward to first visible line
4753 const char *s = text_begin;
4754 if (y + line_height < clip_rect.y)
4755 while (y + line_height < clip_rect.y && s < text_end)
4756 {
4757 const char *line_end = (const char *)ImMemchr(s, '\n', text_end - s);
4758 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4759 {
4760 // FIXME-OPT: This is not optimal as do first do a search for \n before calling CalcWordWrapPositionA().
4761 // If the specs for CalcWordWrapPositionA() were reworked to optionally return on \n we could combine
4762 // both. However it is still better than nothing performing the fast-forward!
4763 s = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, line_end ? line_end : text_end, wrap_width);
4764 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end);
4765 }
4766 else
4767 {
4768 s = line_end ? line_end + 1 : text_end;
4769 }
4770 y += line_height;
4771 }
4772
4773 // For large text, scan for the last visible line in order to avoid over-reserving in the call to PrimReserve()
4774 // Note that very large horizontal line will still be affected by the issue (e.g. a one megabyte string buffer
4775 // without a newline will likely crash atm)
4776 if (text_end - s > 10000 && !word_wrap_enabled)
4777 {
4778 const char *s_end = s;
4779 float y_end = y;
4780 while (y_end < clip_rect.w && s_end < text_end)
4781 {
4782 s_end = (const char *)ImMemchr(s_end, '\n', text_end - s_end);
4783 s_end = s_end ? s_end + 1 : text_end;
4784 y_end += line_height;
4785 }
4786 text_end = s_end;
4787 }
4788 if (s == text_end)
4789 return;
4790
4791 // Reserve vertices for remaining worse case (over-reserving is useful and easily amortized)
4792 const int vtx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 4;
4793 const int idx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 6;
4794 const int idx_expected_size = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + idx_count_max;
4795 draw_list->PrimReserve(idx_count_max, vtx_count_max);
4796 ImDrawVert *vtx_write = draw_list->_VtxWritePtr;
4797 ImDrawIdx *idx_write = draw_list->_IdxWritePtr;
4798 unsigned int vtx_index = draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx;
4799
4800 const ImU32 col_untinted = col | ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
4801 const char *word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4802
4803 while (s < text_end)
4804 {
4805 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4806 {
4807 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not
4808 // intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
4809 if (!word_wrap_eol)
4810 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - (x - origin_x));
4811
4812 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
4813 {
4814 x = origin_x;
4815 y += line_height;
4816 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4817 break; // break out of main loop
4818 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4819 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
4820 continue;
4821 }
4822 }
4823
4824 // Decode and advance source
4825 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4826 if (c < 0x80)
4827 s += 1;
4828 else
4829 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4830
4831 if (c < 32)
4832 {
4833 if (c == '\n')
4834 {
4835 x = origin_x;
4836 y += line_height;
4837 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4838 break; // break out of main loop
4839 continue;
4840 }
4841 if (c == '\r')
4842 continue;
4843 }
4844
4845 const ImFontGlyph *glyph = FindGlyph((ImWchar)c);
4846 if (glyph == NULL)
4847 continue;
4848
4849 float char_width = glyph->AdvanceX * scale;
4850 if (glyph->Visible)
4851 {
4852 // We don't do a second finer clipping test on the Y axis as we've already skipped anything before
4853 // clip_rect.y and exit once we pass clip_rect.w
4854 float x1 = x + glyph->X0 * scale;
4855 float x2 = x + glyph->X1 * scale;
4856 float y1 = y + glyph->Y0 * scale;
4857 float y2 = y + glyph->Y1 * scale;
4858 if (x1 <= clip_rect.z && x2 >= clip_rect.x)
4859 {
4860 // Render a character
4861 float u1 = glyph->U0;
4862 float v1 = glyph->V0;
4863 float u2 = glyph->U1;
4864 float v2 = glyph->V1;
4865
4866 // CPU side clipping used to fit text in their frame when the frame is too small. Only does clipping for
4867 // axis aligned quads.
4868 if (cpu_fine_clip)
4869 {
4870 if (x1 < clip_rect.x)
4871 {
4872 u1 = u1 + (1.0f - (x2 - clip_rect.x) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4873 x1 = clip_rect.x;
4874 }
4875 if (y1 < clip_rect.y)
4876 {
4877 v1 = v1 + (1.0f - (y2 - clip_rect.y) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4878 y1 = clip_rect.y;
4879 }
4880 if (x2 > clip_rect.z)
4881 {
4882 u2 = u1 + ((clip_rect.z - x1) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4883 x2 = clip_rect.z;
4884 }
4885 if (y2 > clip_rect.w)
4886 {
4887 v2 = v1 + ((clip_rect.w - y1) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4888 y2 = clip_rect.w;
4889 }
4890 if (y1 >= y2)
4891 {
4892 x += char_width;
4893 continue;
4894 }
4895 }
4896
4897 // Support for untinted glyphs
4898 ImU32 glyph_col = glyph->Colored ? col_untinted : col;
4899
4900 // We are NOT calling PrimRectUV() here because non-inlined causes too much overhead in a debug builds.
4901 // Inlined here:
4902 {
4903 vtx_write[0].pos.x = x1;
4904 vtx_write[0].pos.y = y1;
4905 vtx_write[0].col = glyph_col;
4906 vtx_write[0].uv.x = u1;
4907 vtx_write[0].uv.y = v1;
4908 vtx_write[1].pos.x = x2;
4909 vtx_write[1].pos.y = y1;
4910 vtx_write[1].col = glyph_col;
4911 vtx_write[1].uv.x = u2;
4912 vtx_write[1].uv.y = v1;
4913 vtx_write[2].pos.x = x2;
4914 vtx_write[2].pos.y = y2;
4915 vtx_write[2].col = glyph_col;
4916 vtx_write[2].uv.x = u2;
4917 vtx_write[2].uv.y = v2;
4918 vtx_write[3].pos.x = x1;
4919 vtx_write[3].pos.y = y2;
4920 vtx_write[3].col = glyph_col;
4921 vtx_write[3].uv.x = u1;
4922 vtx_write[3].uv.y = v2;
4923 idx_write[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index);
4924 idx_write[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 1);
4925 idx_write[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2);
4926 idx_write[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index);
4927 idx_write[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2);
4928 idx_write[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 3);
4929 vtx_write += 4;
4930 vtx_index += 4;
4931 idx_write += 6;
4932 }
4933 }
4934 }
4935 x += char_width;
4936 }
4937
4938 // Give back unused vertices (clipped ones, blanks) ~ this is essentially a PrimUnreserve() action.
4939 draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size = (int)(vtx_write - draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data); // Same as calling shrink()
4940 draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size = (int)(idx_write - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data);
4941 draw_list->CmdBuffer[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1].ElemCount -= (idx_expected_size - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
4942 draw_list->_VtxWritePtr = vtx_write;
4943 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
4944 draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx = vtx_index;
4945}

4947//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4948// [SECTION] ImGui Internal Render Helpers
4949//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

4951// - RenderArrow()

4954// - RenderArrowDockMenu()
4955// - RenderArrowPointingAt()

4962
4963// Render an arrow aimed to be aligned with text (p_min is a position in the same space text would be positioned). To
4964// e.g. denote expanded/collapsed state
4965void ImGui::RenderArrow(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, ImGuiDir dir, float scale)
4966{
4967 const float h = draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 1.00f;
4968 float r = h * 0.40f * scale;
4969 ImVec2 center = pos + ImVec2(h * 0.50f, h * 0.50f * scale);
4970
4971 ImVec2 a, b, c;
4972 switch (dir)
4973 {
4974 case ImGuiDir_Up:
4975 case ImGuiDir_Down:
4976 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Up)
4977 r = -r;
4978 a = ImVec2(+0.000f, +0.750f) * r;
4979 b = ImVec2(-0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4980 c = ImVec2(+0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4981 break;
4982 case ImGuiDir_Left:
4983 case ImGuiDir_Right:
4984 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Left)
4985 r = -r;
4986 a = ImVec2(+0.750f, +0.000f) * r;
4987 b = ImVec2(-0.750f, +0.866f) * r;
4988 c = ImVec2(-0.750f, -0.866f) * r;
4989 break;
4990 case ImGuiDir_None:
4991 case ImGuiDir_COUNT:
4992 IM_ASSERT(0);
4993 break;
4994 }
4995 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(center + a, center + b, center + c, col);
4996}
4997
4998void ImGui::RenderBullet(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col)
4999{
5000 // FIXME-OPT: This should be baked in font.
5001 draw_list->AddCircleFilled(pos, draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 0.20f, col, 8);
5002}
5003
5004void ImGui::RenderCheckMark(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, float sz)
5005{
5006 float thickness = ImMax(sz / 5.0f, 1.0f);
5007 sz -= thickness * 0.5f;
5008 pos += ImVec2(thickness * 0.25f, thickness * 0.25f);
5009
5010 float third = sz / 3.0f;
5011 float bx = pos.x + third;
5012 float by = pos.y + sz - third * 0.5f;
5013 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx - third, by - third));
5014 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx, by));
5015 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx + third * 2.0f, by - third * 2.0f));
5016 draw_list->PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
5017}

5019// Render an arrow. 'pos' is position of the arrow tip. half_sz.x is length from base to tip. half_sz.y is length on
5020// each side.
5021void ImGui::RenderArrowPointingAt(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImVec2 half_sz, ImGuiDir direction, ImU32 col)
5022{
5023 switch (direction)
5024 {
5025 case ImGuiDir_Left:
5026 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y),
5027 ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col);
5028 return;
5029 case ImGuiDir_Right:
5030 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y),
5031 ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col);
5032 return;
5033 case ImGuiDir_Up:
5034 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y),
5035 ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col);
5036 return;
5037 case ImGuiDir_Down:
5038 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y),
5039 ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col);
5040 return;
5041 case ImGuiDir_None:
5042 case ImGuiDir_COUNT:
5043 break; // Fix warnings
5044 }
5045}

5047// This is less wide than RenderArrow() and we use in dock nodes instead of the regular RenderArrow() to denote a change
5048// of functionality, and because the saved space means that the left-most tab label can stay at exactly the same
5049// position as the label of a loose window.
5050void ImGui::RenderArrowDockMenu(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, float sz, ImU32 col)
5051{
5052 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.20f, sz * 0.15f), p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.80f, sz * 0.30f), col);
5053 RenderArrowPointingAt(draw_list, p_min + ImVec2(sz * 0.50f, sz * 0.85f), ImVec2(sz * 0.30f, sz * 0.40f),
5054 ImGuiDir_Down, col);
5055}
5056
5057static inline float ImAcos01(float x)
5058{
5059 if (x <= 0.0f)
5060 return IM_PI * 0.5f;
5061 if (x >= 1.0f)
5062 return 0.0f;
5063 return ImAcos(x);
5064 // return (-0.69813170079773212f * x * x - 0.87266462599716477f) * x + 1.5707963267948966f; // Cheap approximation,
5065 // may be enough for what we do.
5066}
5067
5068// FIXME: Cleanup and move code to ImDrawList.
5069void ImGui::RenderRectFilledRangeH(ImDrawList *draw_list, const ImRect &rect, ImU32 col, float x_start_norm,
5070 float x_end_norm, float rounding)
5071{
5072 if (x_end_norm == x_start_norm)
5073 return;
5074 if (x_start_norm > x_end_norm)
5075 ImSwap(x_start_norm, x_end_norm);
5076
5077 ImVec2 p0 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_start_norm), rect.Min.y);
5078 ImVec2 p1 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_end_norm), rect.Max.y);
5079 if (rounding == 0.0f)
5080 {
5081 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p0, p1, col, 0.0f);
5082 return;
5083 }
5084
5085 rounding =
5086 ImClamp(ImMin((rect.Max.x - rect.Min.x) * 0.5f, (rect.Max.y - rect.Min.y) * 0.5f) - 1.0f, 0.0f, rounding);
5087 const float inv_rounding = 1.0f / rounding;
5088 const float arc0_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p0.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
5089 const float arc0_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p1.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
5090 const float half_pi =
5091 IM_PI * 0.5f; // We will == compare to this because we know this is the exact value ImAcos01 can return.
5092 const float x0 = ImMax(p0.x, rect.Min.x + rounding);
5093 if (arc0_b == arc0_e)
5094 {
5095 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y));
5096 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y));
5097 }
5098 else if (arc0_b == 0.0f && arc0_e == half_pi)
5099 {
5100 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 3, 6); // BL
5101 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 6, 9); // TR
5102 }
5103 else
5104 {
5105 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, IM_PI - arc0_e, IM_PI - arc0_b); // BL
5106 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, IM_PI + arc0_b, IM_PI + arc0_e); // TR
5107 }
5108 if (p1.x > rect.Min.x + rounding)
5109 {
5110 const float arc1_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p1.x) * inv_rounding);
5111 const float arc1_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p0.x) * inv_rounding);
5112 const float x1 = ImMin(p1.x, rect.Max.x - rounding);
5113 if (arc1_b == arc1_e)
5114 {
5115 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y));
5116 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y));
5117 }
5118 else if (arc1_b == 0.0f && arc1_e == half_pi)
5119 {
5120 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 9, 12); // TR
5121 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 0, 3); // BR
5122 }
5123 else
5124 {
5125 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, -arc1_e, -arc1_b); // TR
5126 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, +arc1_b, +arc1_e); // BR
5127 }
5128 }
5129 draw_list->PathFillConvex(col);
5130}
5131
5132void ImGui::RenderRectFilledWithHole(ImDrawList *draw_list, const ImRect &outer, const ImRect &inner, ImU32 col,
5133 float rounding)
5134{
5135 const bool fill_L = (inner.Min.x > outer.Min.x);
5136 const bool fill_R = (inner.Max.x < outer.Max.x);
5137 const bool fill_U = (inner.Min.y > outer.Min.y);
5138 const bool fill_D = (inner.Max.y < outer.Max.y);
5139 if (fill_L)
5140 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding,
5141 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) |
5142 (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft));
5143 if (fill_R)
5144 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding,
5145 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) |
5146 (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
5147 if (fill_U)
5148 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding,
5149 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) |
5150 (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight));
5151 if (fill_D)
5152 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding,
5153 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) |
5154 (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
5155 if (fill_L && fill_U)
5156 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding,
5157 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft);
5158 if (fill_R && fill_U)
5159 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding,
5160 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight);
5161 if (fill_L && fill_D)
5162 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding,
5163 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft);
5164 if (fill_R && fill_D)
5165 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding,
5166 ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight);
5167}
5168
5169ImDrawFlags ImGui::CalcRoundingFlagsForRectInRect(const ImRect &r_in, const ImRect &r_outer, float threshold)
5170{
5171 bool round_l = r_in.Min.x <= r_outer.Min.x + threshold;
5172 bool round_r = r_in.Max.x >= r_outer.Max.x - threshold;
5173 bool round_t = r_in.Min.y <= r_outer.Min.y + threshold;
5174 bool round_b = r_in.Max.y >= r_outer.Max.y - threshold;
5175 return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | ((round_t && round_l) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft : 0) |
5176 ((round_t && round_r) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight : 0) |
5177 ((round_b && round_l) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft : 0) |
5178 ((round_b && round_r) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight : 0);
5179}
5180
5181// Helper for ColorPicker4()
5182// NB: This is rather brittle and will show artifact when rounding this enabled if rounded corners overlap multiple
5183// cells. Caller currently responsible for avoiding that. Spent a non reasonable amount of time trying to getting this
5184// right for ColorButton with rounding+anti-aliasing+ImGuiColorEditFlags_HalfAlphaPreview flag + various grid sizes and
5185// offsets, and eventually gave up... probably more reasonable to disable rounding altogether.
5186// FIXME: uses ImGui::GetColorU32
5187void ImGui::RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard(ImDrawList *draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, ImVec2 p_max, ImU32 col,
5188 float grid_step, ImVec2 grid_off, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
5189{
5190 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
5191 flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersDefault_;
5192 if (((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) >> IM_COL32_A_SHIFT) < 0xFF)
5193 {
5194 ImU32 col_bg1 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(204, 204, 204, 255), col));
5195 ImU32 col_bg2 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(128, 128, 128, 255), col));
5196 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col_bg1, rounding, flags);
5197
5198 int yi = 0;
5199 for (float y = p_min.y + grid_off.y; y < p_max.y; y += grid_step, yi++)
5200 {
5201 float y1 = ImClamp(y, p_min.y, p_max.y), y2 = ImMin(y + grid_step, p_max.y);
5202 if (y2 <= y1)
5203 continue;
5204 for (float x = p_min.x + grid_off.x + (yi & 1) * grid_step; x < p_max.x; x += grid_step * 2.0f)
5205 {
5206 float x1 = ImClamp(x, p_min.x, p_max.x), x2 = ImMin(x + grid_step, p_max.x);
5207 if (x2 <= x1)
5208 continue;
5209 ImDrawFlags cell_flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone;
5210 if (y1 <= p_min.y)
5211 {
5212 if (x1 <= p_min.x)
5213 cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft;
5214 if (x2 >= p_max.x)
5215 cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight;
5216 }
5217 if (y2 >= p_max.y)
5218 {
5219 if (x1 <= p_min.x)
5220 cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft;
5221 if (x2 >= p_max.x)
5222 cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight;
5223 }
5224
5225 // Combine flags
5226 cell_flags = (flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone || cell_flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
5227 ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone
5228 : (cell_flags & flags);
5229 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(x1, y1), ImVec2(x2, y2), col_bg2, rounding, cell_flags);
5230 }
5231 }
5232 }
5233 else
5234 {
5235 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col, rounding, flags);
5236 }
5237}
5238
5239//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
5240// [SECTION] Decompression code
5241//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
5242// Compressed with stb_compress() then converted to a C array and encoded as base85.
5243// Use the program in misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp to create the array from a TTF file.
5244// The purpose of encoding as base85 instead of "0x00,0x01,..." style is only save on _source code_ size.
5245// Decompression from stb.h (public domain) by Sean Barrett https://github.com/nothings/stb/blob/master/stb.h
5246//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
5247
5248static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char *input)
5249{
5250 return (input[8] << 24) + (input[9] << 16) + (input[10] << 8) + input[11];
5251}
5252
5253static unsigned char *stb__barrier_out_e, *stb__barrier_out_b;
5254static const unsigned char *stb__barrier_in_b;
5255static unsigned char *stb__dout;
5256static void stb__match(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
5257{
5258 // INVERSE of memmove... write each byte before copying the next...
5259 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
5260 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e)
5261 {
5262 stb__dout += length;
5263 return;
5264 }
5265 if (data < stb__barrier_out_b)
5266 {
5267 stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e + 1;
5268 return;
5269 }
5270 while (length--)
5271 *stb__dout++ = *data++;
5272}
5273
5274static void stb__lit(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
5275{
5276 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
5277 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e)
5278 {
5279 stb__dout += length;
5280 return;
5281 }
5282 if (data < stb__barrier_in_b)
5283 {
5284 stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e + 1;
5285 return;
5286 }
5287 memcpy(stb__dout, data, length);
5288 stb__dout += length;
5289}
5290
5291#define stb__in2(x) ((i[x] << 8) + i[(x) + 1])
5292#define stb__in3(x) ((i[x] << 16) + stb__in2((x) + 1))
5293#define stb__in4(x) ((i[x] << 24) + stb__in3((x) + 1))
5294
5295static const unsigned char *stb_decompress_token(const unsigned char *i)
5296{
5297 if (*i >= 0x20)
5298 { // use fewer if's for cases that expand small
5299 if (*i >= 0x80)
5300 stb__match(stb__dout - i[1] - 1, i[0] - 0x80 + 1), i += 2;
5301 else if (*i >= 0x40)
5302 stb__match(stb__dout - (stb__in2(0) - 0x4000 + 1), i[2] + 1), i += 3;
5303 else /* *i >= 0x20 */
5304 stb__lit(i + 1, i[0] - 0x20 + 1), i += 1 + (i[0] - 0x20 + 1);
5305 }
5306 else
5307 { // more ifs for cases that expand large, since overhead is amortized
5308 if (*i >= 0x18)
5309 stb__match(stb__dout - (stb__in3(0) - 0x180000 + 1), i[3] + 1), i += 4;
5310 else if (*i >= 0x10)
5311 stb__match(stb__dout - (stb__in3(0) - 0x100000 + 1), stb__in2(3) + 1), i += 5;
5312 else if (*i >= 0x08)
5313 stb__lit(i + 2, stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1), i += 2 + (stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1);
5314 else if (*i == 0x07)
5315 stb__lit(i + 3, stb__in2(1) + 1), i += 3 + (stb__in2(1) + 1);
5316 else if (*i == 0x06)
5317 stb__match(stb__dout - (stb__in3(1) + 1), i[4] + 1), i += 5;
5318 else if (*i == 0x04)
5319 stb__match(stb__dout - (stb__in3(1) + 1), stb__in2(4) + 1), i += 6;
5320 }
5321 return i;
5322}
5323
5324static unsigned int stb_adler32(unsigned int adler32, unsigned char *buffer, unsigned int buflen)
5325{
5326 const unsigned long ADLER_MOD = 65521;
5327 unsigned long s1 = adler32 & 0xffff, s2 = adler32 >> 16;
5328 unsigned long blocklen = buflen % 5552;
5329
5330 unsigned long i;
5331 while (buflen)
5332 {
5333 for (i = 0; i + 7 < blocklen; i += 8)
5334 {
5335 s1 += buffer[0], s2 += s1;
5336 s1 += buffer[1], s2 += s1;
5337 s1 += buffer[2], s2 += s1;
5338 s1 += buffer[3], s2 += s1;
5339 s1 += buffer[4], s2 += s1;
5340 s1 += buffer[5], s2 += s1;
5341 s1 += buffer[6], s2 += s1;
5342 s1 += buffer[7], s2 += s1;
5343
5344 buffer += 8;
5345 }
5346
5347 for (; i < blocklen; ++i)
5348 s1 += *buffer++, s2 += s1;
5349
5350 s1 %= ADLER_MOD, s2 %= ADLER_MOD;
5351 buflen -= blocklen;
5352 blocklen = 5552;
5353 }
5354 return (unsigned int)(s2 << 16) + (unsigned int)s1;
5355}
5356
5357static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char *output, const unsigned char *i, unsigned int /*length*/)
5358{
5359 if (stb__in4(0) != 0x57bC0000)
5360 return 0;
5361 if (stb__in4(4) != 0)
5362 return 0; // error! stream is > 4GB
5363 const unsigned int olen = stb_decompress_length(i);
5364 stb__barrier_in_b = i;
5365 stb__barrier_out_e = output + olen;
5366 stb__barrier_out_b = output;
5367 i += 16;
5368
5369 stb__dout = output;
5370 for (;;)
5371 {
5372 const unsigned char *old_i = i;
5373 i = stb_decompress_token(i);
5374 if (i == old_i)
5375 {
5376 if (*i == 0x05 && i[1] == 0xfa)
5377 {
5378 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout == output + olen);
5379 if (stb__dout != output + olen)
5380 return 0;
5381 if (stb_adler32(1, output, olen) != (unsigned int)stb__in4(2))
5382 return 0;
5383 return olen;
5384 }
5385 else
5386 {
5387 IM_ASSERT(0); /* NOTREACHED */
5388 return 0;
5389 }
5390 }
5391 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout <= output + olen);
5392 if (stb__dout > output + olen)
5393 return 0;
5394 }
5395}
